    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });

  <span id="freeText16806571546609721715" style="display:none"><i>Note to Self<br /><br />Love is patient; love is kind.<br />Love doesn't boast or brag.<br />There's no arrogance in love;<br />it's never rude, crude, or indecent-it's not self absorbed.<br />Love isn't easily upset.<br />Love doesn't tally wrongs.<br />Love trusts, hopes, and endures no matter what.<br />Love will never become obsolete.<br />I'll fight for her.<br /><br />Thief</i><br /><br />Caleb Drake never got over his first love. Not when he got married. Not when she got married. When life suddenly comes full circle Caleb must decide how far he is willing to go to get the aloof and alluring Olivia Kaspen back. But for every action in life there is a consequence, and soon Caleb finds out that sometimes love comes at an unbearably high price.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/436337752?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12821757-zizz?shelf=absolute">absolute</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer436337752" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2791574200695816124">At 89% (loc 3059), Olivia talks of that fateful day when she decided to go back to the music store to talk to Caleb as opposed to leaving with Dobson. <br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I've never told anyone but,that moment - that one, every-changing moment - <u>has made a profound impact on me.</u></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <u>This runs parallel to my life and most likely to hundreds (if not thousands) of us.</u>
</b> I was busy in real life and was content in my reading cave for one. I became unglued after TO. Scoured the web for any piece of scrap that c</span>
  <span id="freeText2791574200695816124" style="display:none">At 89% (loc 3059), Olivia talks of that fateful day when she decided to go back to the music store to talk to Caleb as opposed to leaving with Dobson. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I've never told anyone but,that moment - that one, every-changing moment - <u>has made a profound impact on me.</u></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><b>
  <u>This runs parallel to my life and most likely to hundreds (if not thousands) of us.</u>
</b> I was busy in real life and was content in my reading cave for one. I became unglued after TO. Scoured the web for any piece of scrap that can help me deal with the hurt. I went and registered for Goodreads, wrote my first ever review, joined Maryse's board, The Pressed Penny and eventually found The TOL group. It turns out I was not alone in my need for therapy. Reading has become a huge part of my life and it has since become a social activity for me. <b>Reading TO has been lifechanging for me that discussing it to death is akin to me discussing children with other mothers in real life.</b> <br /><br />It was the perfect mix of various things: Tarryn's excellent writing; the holes in the story that kept you on edge and guessing (going crazy most of the time); the general feeling of impending doom the book makes you feel right from that very first page; the twists and turns that mirror the list here of the 10 craziest roads on earth (<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.environmentalgraffiti.com/cities/news-wacky-roads-around-world);">http://www.environmentalgraffiti.com/...</a> and that devastation at the end. I've read a few sad endings but TO's ending was the closest I ever came to re-living my first heartbreak. <b>I'm an avid reader but I read books and move on. Yet, almost a year later, here I am still obsessed with Caleb and Olivia's story. </b><br /><br /><b>I needed my closure. <br />I needed Caleb to redeem himself. <br />I needed the holes in the story to be satisfactorily plugged in. <br />Most off all I needed Caleb and Olivia to end up together complete with an epilogue that shows me these characters years from now - healthy, happy and most importantly together. </b><br /><br /><b><u>TARRYN FISHER DOES NOT DISAPPOINT IN THIEF. IT IS EVERYTHING YOU CAN HOPE FOR AND SO MUCH MORE.</u><br /><br />Warning: Spoilers ahead</b><br /><br />This is more than a love story. <b>This is a testament to a love that is so profound that it never goes away. <i>"It can never be put to rest because it kept coming back to haunt them.</i></b> Years pass. Grave mistakes are made. Other people get in the way. Casualties litter the place. Yet Olivia and Caleb always go back to each other. It is the kind of love <i>"that can stain your soul, make you beg not to have one, just to escape the spell...It was as if I breathed a spore of her into my lungs...We kept coming back to each other. The distance between our bodies grew wider over the years as we tried to live separately. But that spore took root and grew. And no matter the distance or circumstance, Olivia is something that grows inside of me."</i><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Olivia. I've lost her three times. The first was to impatience. The second was to a lie so dense we couldn't work our way through it, and the third time - this time - I've lost her to Noah."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />I had high hopes given the title and that amazing blurb. But in keeping with Tarryn's style, heart-aching twists continued in the final installment of this saga. It didn't go where I expected it to go. I basically expected Caleb to go after her immediately from that birthday party we had glimpsed in DR. BUT NO. For the first 18%, I wanted to smack Caleb upside the head for giving up so easily as always. My exact thoughts were "Well, so much for fighting for her." <i>"And I don't hear from her for another year."</i> Are you f*cking kidding me Caleb? After a decade, you let a year pass and she had to call you?! I almost had a conniption. And at 7%, I think I actually had a minor stroke. <br /> <br />BUT Caleb, the man we love to hate, <b>REDEEMS HIMSELF FULLY in Thief</b>. We are witnesses to how deep his love runs for Olivia.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Let me carry you out. I'll never let you touch the ground. I was made to carry you, Olivia. You're fucking heavy with all of your guilt and self-loathing. But I can do it. Because I love you."<br />"I want your babies, and your anger, and your cold blue eyes. I want to go on anniversary dinners with you, I want to wrap Christmas presents with you. I want to fight with you about stupid things and then hold you down in my bed and make it up to you. I want to have more cake batter fights and camping trips. I want your future, Olivia. Please come back to me." </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Caleb eventually gets it - with two marriages between them and Estella.<br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> "How is it that you always let me go easily then? Why don't you know that I want you to fight for me?"<br /><br />"It took me a long time to figure out that's what you were saying...But ten years later, here I am. Fighting. I'd like to think I've learned from my mistakes. I'd also like to think we've finally made it to the point where we are ready for each other...Maybe this is finally our time. Maybe."<br /><br />"So, I fight. That's it. That's my only option. And if I don't get her, If she doesn't choose me. I'm going to be that guy - who spends his life alone and pining. Because I sure as hell am not going to replace her with any more Leahs or Jessicas or any-goddamn-body-else...It's Olivia or nothing."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />Unfortunately, Olivia wants to live right by Noah. And she was afraid of Caleb hurting her again. <br /><br />But as has been the case repeatedly in the past decade, Caleb and Olivia EVENTUALLY come back to each other again. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Eventually. That word is so us, isn't it?...Eventually, we'll come back together, fall apart, come back together."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><b>It is kismet. They are soulmates.</b> <br /><br />But we do not get our rainbows and unicorns. This is not the truth this series has delivered from the very beginning. The ending is bittersweet. Sad but not tragic. They had hurt people and perhaps this is karma. They had to live with the consequences of so much time wasted. <br /><br /><b>BUT THEIR LOVE HEALS. OLIVIA LIKENS IT TO A GOD-GIVEN TOOL THAT SCREWS THINGS BACK IN PLACE. IT FIXES THEM.</b><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"We are gonna be okay. That's what happens when two people are meant. You just work it out until you are okay. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><b>THIS IS ONE OF THE MOST BEAUTIFUL, POWERFUL AND CAPTIVATING LOVE STORIES I'VE EVER READ. ONE THAT WILL HAUNT ME FOREVER. For me, it is the most emotionally gratifying closure that I could have ever hoped for. And somehow I find that it has helped fixed that part of myself too - the one that became unglued almost a year ago after reading The Opportunist.<br /><br />I am overwhelmed. I am beyond happy - in spite of... My heart is overflowing with emotions YET I feel so light as if a heavy burden has been lifted off me. I haven't picked up a book for a week now. And I have no desire to move on. I want to savor this. I am so grateful for Tarryn Fisher for sharing Caleb and Olivia's story with us. They are flawed and imperfect. But they are perfect for each other. The end is perfect in its imperfections.<br /><br />What else is there to say except that Tarryn Fisher is one of the best - if not the absolute best - among indie authors.</b> <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2791574200695816124" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_672208771" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/672208771" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/672208771?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer672208771" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11069663326730297203"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429835i/861405.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429835i/861406._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ***<br/><br/><b> Woah. I'm still reeling here. <br/><br/>Caleb and Olivia have one of the most heart-breakingly dysfunctional and yet achingly beautiful love stories I've ever read. </b><br/><br/>They had an irreplaceable love proved unbreakable even by a lifetime of mistakes. They were destructive, made the wrong choices and paid the painful price for their mistakes but you couldn't help but root for them every step of the way.  Their journey was an intense, heartbreaking, non-stop roller coaster filled </span>
  <span id="freeText11069663326730297203" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429835i/861405.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429835i/861406._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ***<br><br><b> Woah. I'm still reeling here. <br><br>Caleb and Olivia have one of the most heart-breakingly dysfunctional and yet achingly beautiful love stories I've ever read. </b><br><br>They had an irreplaceable love proved unbreakable even by a lifetime of mistakes. They were destructive, made the wrong choices and paid the painful price for their mistakes but you couldn't help but root for them every step of the way.  Their journey was an intense, heartbreaking, non-stop roller coaster filled to the brim with every possible emotion you can imagine.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"She’s mine. She always has been, she always will be. We’ve been running in opposite directions for the last ten years, and we collide at every turn. Sometimes it’s because we’re looking for each other, other times it’s fate.</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>She has the kind of love that can stain your soul, make you beg not to have one, just to escape the spell she’s put you under. I’ve tried to break myself of her over and over, but it’s pointless. I’ve got more of her in my veins than blood… </em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>We're not over. We'll never be over."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The truth of is that this is a second-chance love story. The difference between this one and the usual ones is that in this story you live through the years of separation and mistakes along with the characters and go through their whole tangled love story with them - start to finish - and because you've been through every moment of heartbreak and pain right along side them, when the happiness shines through you value it so much more and can appreciate it with every part of your heart and soul because you *know* the price they paid for it.<br><br>My heart was racing with anticipation from the very first line of this book. This was IT. It was really happening. The last hurdle. And <em>what</em> an incredible opening chapter!!! One of the very best!<br><br>Because of the way this story had built from the first book, I really felt like I had lived these characters lives with them. Their memories were my memories. Little things like "<em>the pool where I first kissed her</em>" came loaded with a whole slew of heart-pounding emotions.<br><br>This book tells Caleb's POV. <em>Finally</em> we get to see what was going on inside his mind. Why did he fall in love with Olivia? Why did he push so hard? Why did he walk away? Why did he waste those 5 years? What made him hurt? What made him love? What drove his actions? And most importantly we see the true depth of how completely and all-consumingly he <em>
  <strong>loved </strong>
</em>Olivia.<br><br>It's like he finally got her. Or maybe he did all along and wasn't ready to admit it. But either way, this was the turning point. He was ready to fight for her.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"I can't stay away from you. I've been trying for ten years."</em>
</blockquote><br>But I won't lie, sometimes it hurt to see the raw honesty of Caleb's thoughts. They were... naked. Uninhibited. Painfully truthful. He was no Boy Scout, that's for sure, but it was impossible not to love him. Flaws, mistakes, imperfections and all.<br><br>As with the first two books, this one wove both the past and present together - starting from flashbacks of when they first met and going through their lives highlighting milestones and key turnings points that, for better or for worse, changed their lives forever. There was no repetitiveness in the flashbacks but rather they gave new insight into everything and filled in the blanks by giving us answers, clarifications and explanations that slowly brought the last broken threads of this story together.<br><br>I absolutely loved that Caleb genuinely loved Olivia for who she was. He wasn't some starry eyed romantic who saw her in a different light just because he was in love with her. No, he saw right <em>into</em> her and he fell in love with her just. as. she. was.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"I tried to break her before. Now, I just wanted her as she was. I wanted every last beautiful flaw. I wanted the witty one-liners and the coldness that only I knew how to warm. I wanted the fight and the friction and the make-up sex. I wanted her to wake up in my bed every morning. I wanted her shitty cooking and her beautiful, complex mind."<br></em>
</blockquote><br>Overall I found this book more sad than angsty, unlike the first two. I'd reached the point where my heart was almost permanently broken. I just wanted them to be happy <em>so badly</em>. I wanted them to be together in more than just their hearts. The weight of it all was almost too much. Too sad. Too heart breaking.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Do you remember the orange grove, Olivia?"</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>And just when I thought things couldn't get sadder, new bombshells of pain were dropped. There were moments so powerfully emotional that I could do nothing other than just sit there and cry.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I want your babies, and your anger, and your cold blue eyes…" I choke on my words and I am the one to look away. I bring my gaze back to her face and realize that if I can't convince her now, I'm never going to be able to. "I want to go on anniversary dinners with you, I want to wrap Christmas presents with you. I want to fight with you about stupid things and then hold you down in my bed and make it up to you. I want to have more cake batter fights and camping trips. I want your future, Olivia. Please come back to me."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Caleb and Olivia were just such a heart-breakingly dysfunctional mess - desperately in love with each other and yet forever ruining their chances of happiness. I don't even have words to describe the frustration and pain.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"How many times can a heart be broken before it is beyond mend?"</em>
</blockquote><br>My heart was yo-yoed with. Toyed with. Trampled. Broken. Shattered. Mended. And broken again.<br><br>The book made me angry. Furious. Frustrated. I wanted to punch the wall, scream at the characters and then just sob into my pillow because I loved them so much and their pain became my pain and their precious moments of happiness became seconds I'd desperately cling to.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <strong>
      <em>"I don’t love anything more than I love you."</em>
    </strong>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I find it interesting that I loved this story as much as I did (5 stars for every book) because even though it was loaded with nearly everything that usually bothers me in books, I still loved and was captivated by every <em>single</em> word of this trilogy. I swear to you, more than half my book is highlighted.<br><br><strong>Tarryn Fisher has a way of making you feel every moment of the story with every piece of your heart.</strong> The writing is just phenomenal. Absolutely phenomenal.<br><br>This book is full of these little beautiful things that are just loaded with memories, meaning and emotion. Airport blue. The penny. The tree. Cherry Garcia. The deflated basket ball. The orange grove. Jaxson's. Duchess. Peter Pan. *sob*<br><br>The ending was bittersweet. Perfect in it's imperfections... just like them.<br><br>I didn't know what to think at first. When I finished (at 3AM, I might add) I actually just sat there on the couch for about an hour staring blankly in front of me processing my various emotions. I needed to come to terms with the story. Then, over an hour later, my heart still heavy and aching, I went back and reread the epilogue and just <em>sobbed</em>. It was like I needed that time to come to terms with it and accept it.<br><br>I loved it. I hated it. I loved it. I hated it. I was mad. Mad at them for their decisions in life. If <em>only</em> they'd just made different choices. They came so close so many times to happiness. The pain and devastation that they brought down on themselves and had to go through over the years gutted me. But their love that held strong throughout all of the pain, the mistakes, the wrong turns. It withstood it all and survived. They survived. Together.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <strong>
      <em> "We are gonna be okay. That's what happens when two people are meant to be. You just work it out until you are okay."</em>
    </strong>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>If you're looking for a fairy tale, this isn't the story for you. Nothing could erase the past. Mistakes were made, wrong turns were taken, and their promise of a better tomorrow would forever be haunted by the ghosts of '<em>what if's' </em>and laced with regret for the past and for missed opportunities they could never get back. There was hope, happiness and healing but it was won at a heavy price. <b> In the end, I was given the things I needed at the cost of the things I wanted. </b><br><br>I have to say though that it was incredibly well done and I seriously commend Tarryn Fisher's brilliant storytelling for this because I think that in the end, we were left feeling exactly how Caleb and Olivia felt.<br><br>They'd had an unconventional romance and so their ending was no different. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They were happy and together at the end and honestly, I couldn't ask for anything more.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> But still, the tears wouldn't stop falling, my heart won't stop aching, and I can promise you that I will never forget this story.<br><br>I'm writing this almost a full 24 hours after finishing the book and I have the book hangover of the century. I can't stop thinking about this story. Pieces of it just keep playing over and over again in my mind.<br><br><b> Flawed. Dysfunctional. Beautiful. <br><br>This is a must-read trilogy! </b><br><br>5 stars!!<br><br>**PLEASE NOTE: <i>Thief</i> is the conclusion to this trilogy. It is 
  <em>not</em>
 a standalone. The three books in this series must be read in order because it's one continuous story. :)<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786137._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429835i/861407._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Now... I almost never use gifs but right when I finished, these described my emotional reaction:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429835ra/861408.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429835ra/861409.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/631154.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298666ra/686643.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/658287.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a><br></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="11069663326730297203" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_436254545" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/436254545" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/436254545?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer436254545" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11104083800973979554"><b>5+ Perfectly Imperfect Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/eb2587b9-daca-46af-9391-864122862236_zps4f4b4436.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394635i/759791.jpg' alt=' photo eb2587b9-daca-46af-9391-864122862236_zps4f4b4436.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I loved this book. I hated this book. I loved this book. I hated this book. I loved this book...<br/><br/>Okay, you get it. Tarryn Fisher can mess with your mind like no other. Her writing is incredible. Her characters are unforgettable. No surprise, this was a 5 star read for me. I would give it more than 5 stars if I could... SO many feelings SO many emotions. I’ve struggled to write this review, collecting your thoughts on a book like this isn’t easy, but here ya go!<br/><br/>Thi</span>
  <span id="freeText11104083800973979554" style="display:none"><b>5+ Perfectly Imperfect Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/eb2587b9-daca-46af-9391-864122862236_zps4f4b4436.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394635i/759791.jpg" alt=" photo eb2587b9-daca-46af-9391-864122862236_zps4f4b4436.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved this book. I hated this book. I loved this book. I hated this book. I loved this book...<br><br>Okay, you get it. Tarryn Fisher can mess with your mind like no other. Her writing is incredible. Her characters are unforgettable. No surprise, this was a 5 star read for me. I would give it more than 5 stars if I could... SO many feelings SO many emotions. I’ve struggled to write this review, collecting your thoughts on a book like this isn’t easy, but here ya go!<br><br>Thief is written mostly all from Caleb’s pov. It takes place ten years after the Opportunist, and has many devastating flashbacks into the past. Everything you wanted to know from <i>The Opportunist</i> and <i>Dirty Red</i>, you get it. Questions get answered, things get clarified. <br><br>Caleb and Olivia have one of the most dysfunctional, fucked up, twisted love stories of all time... And I love it! While reading this, your heart will hurt. Seriously. You may laugh, you will cry, you won’t know how to feel. Don’t worry, that is a normal reaction for one of Tarryn’s books. This book will captivate you from the first word until the last. The writing is brilliant, spectacular.<br><br>What does it mean to <i>‘do the right thing?’.</i> Is it the right thing what is best for others, whats best for your self, what society deems best? Is being selfish wrong, or is it right sometimes? What if whats right for one person isn’t right for another? <br><br>Caleb Drake has always wanted to do the right thing, but the right thing for whom? He’s lived, he’s learned, he’s doing what <i>he</i> has to do now, whether it’s right or wrong. I’m just going to throw this out there quickly... In my eyes, Caleb is perfect. This book just solidified that.<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’ve come to the conclusion that there are no set rules in life. You do what you have to do to survive. If that means running away from the love of your life to preserve your sanity, you do it. If it means breaking someone’s heart so yours doesn’t break; do it. Life is complicated — too much so for there to be absolutes.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/7097d143-836e-4cc1-a048-2246bcd284ea_zps79251ccd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394635i/759792.jpg" alt=" photo 7097d143-836e-4cc1-a048-2246bcd284ea_zps79251ccd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> Caleb has been in love one time and one time only. To Olivia Kaspen. Ten years ago, he fell in love under a tree and has never been the same again. He’s been married to an evil bitch, she is still married, life has not been kind to either of them. Every chance they had to be together got screwed up some way or another. Not this time. Caleb has to have Olivia. If he can’t have her, he wants no one. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“She’s mine. She always has been, she always will be.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/d39258f0-a07f-4215-a030-4c6c335e3831_zps315e891f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394635i/759793.jpg" alt=" photo d39258f0-a07f-4215-a030-4c6c335e3831_zps315e891f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Lies, it sounds demented to want a woman’s lies. But, Olivia loves you with her lies. She lies about how she’s feeling, how she’s hurting, how she wants you when she tells you she doesn’t. She lies to protect you and herself.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Caleb doesn’t care what he has to do. This time, he is fighting for Olivia. That the final installment of this fantastic series was written from Caleb’s p.o.v. was the icing on the cake. I needed to know what happened in the past from his perspective. Caleb has always been in love with Olivia. All the things he did in the last two books, mistakes he made, he had his reasons. Caleb will do anything to get Olivia back. Anything. He makes that very clear to her.<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I'll do whatever I have to do to protect you. I'll lie, cheat, and steal to make you okay. I'll share your suffering, and I'll carry you when you're weighed down. I'll never leave you, not even when you ask me to. Do you believe me?”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>There are so many obstacles in the way of Caleb’s happiness. Noah is obstacle number one. With the problems he and Olivia are having, the game changes a bit. Leah is also a huge obstacle. I would love to say that the crazy, dirty bitch stayed away and didn’t cause any trouble this book, but I would be lying. <br><br>I don’t wan to go into to much detail over the story line. So much happens, you don’t want it spoiled. One thing is certain, prepare for another mind fuck...<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/Thief-Mindfuck_zpsbae4e575.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394635i/759794.jpg" alt=" photo Thief-Mindfuck_zpsbae4e575.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>You will have all kinds of feelings and you won’t know what to do with them. <br> Sometimes, when you fall in love with some one, truly fall in love, you never fall out. No matter what happens, who else you are with, makes no difference. That person is in your heart, your blood, you couldn’t get them out if you tried. Olivia and Caleb have that kind of love. They fell in love once, under a tree, and they’ve never truly fallen out. Neither one. No matter where life took them, who else they may have loved, it could never compare to this once in a lifetime kind of love. <br><b>
  <blockquote>‘I don’t love anything more than I love you.’</blockquote>
</b> <br> I highlighted the mess out of this book. I am going to share <i>some</i> of my favorite quotes:<br><i>
  <blockquote>“Maybe our souls touched underneath that tree. Maybe I decided to love her. Maybe love wasn't our choice. But when I looked at that woman, I saw myself differently.”<br><br>“She will be your destruction. She's not healthy."<br>"Then let her destroy me.”<br><br>“That was the exact moment my heart threaded with hers. It was as if someone reached down with a sewing needle and stitched my soul to hers. How could one woman be so sharp and so vulnerable at the same time? Whatever would happen to her would happen to me. Whatever pain she would feel, I would feel it too. I wanted it — that was the surprising part. Selfish, self centered Caleb Drake loved a girl so much he could already feel himself changing to accommodate her needs.<br>I fell. <br>Hard.<br>For the rest of this life and probably the next.<br>I wanted her — every last inch of her stubborn, combative, catty heart.”<br><br>‘You’re strong. Strong enough to protect your heart and mine, and your heart from mine. I’ll give you everything I have because from the day I met you, it’s belonged to you.’<br><br>“Life does not accommodate you, it shatters you. Love is mean, but it’s good. It keeps us alive.” <br><br>‘We’re not over. We’ll never be over.’</blockquote>
</i><br><br>This was a crazy, intense and emotional ride. Heartbreaking. You love these characters, you hate these characters, they are a mess. They are flawed, broken, self-centered, yet beautiful. These characters are far from perfect, but they are real. There is a lot of growth from both Caleb and Olivia in this book. The lies, the truth, the drama, angst, everything about this book is amazing. <br><br>The ending. In it was as good as it was going to get for this author. I don’t want to spoil it, I was happy enough. Tarryn stayed true to herself and her characters. Could a few different things made it better, sure. Could it have been worse- hell yes. I’m not going to complain. After finishing this book, I was happy enough. I was satisfied. The epilogue left me in tears. My book hangover is like no other. <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> We are gonna be okay. That’s what happens when two people are meant. You just work it out until you are okay.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>This book is so compelling, once you start it don’t expect to be able to put it down. <br><br>There are things about this series I will never forget. The tree. The penny. Cherry Garcia. Peter Pan. Airport Blue. Duchess. This is a phenomenal and unforgettable series. If you haven’t read it, now that all 3 books are out, you have no reason not to! One of the most consuming, well written series I have ever had the pleasure of reading. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/ef8d81fd-10f0-4313-836a-7663fea0d5bc_zps21381151.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394635i/759795.jpg" alt=" photo ef8d81fd-10f0-4313-836a-7663fea0d5bc_zps21381151.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Broken people give broken love. And we are all a little broken. You just have to forgive and sew up the wounds love delivers, and move on.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="11104083800973979554" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer6068290110508988371">This review contains SPOILERS.<br/><br/>THIS. BOOK.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759767.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mm1neoe5B21s9wbrao1_500_zps454dcd46.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I don't really know what to say...<br/><br/>This book was everything I wanted, everything I hated, something that I loved and well as you can see I am a wreck on the emotional scale.<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759768.gif' alt=' photo emotionalgif2_zps20f92d89.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><u>The Characters</u><br/><br/><b>Leah was all</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759769.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_inline_mpd8m5Zd0k1qz4rgp_zps40ccfa11.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>And Olivia was like</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759770.gif' alt=' photo reallybitch.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759771.gif' alt=' photo IdontgiveaF_zps4bbde43c.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>Leah could not accept this...so she was all</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759772.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_inline_mpd8knBvHl1qz4rgp_zps5ca70318.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>Meanwhile Caleb was allll about winning Olivia back</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759773.gif' alt=' photo iloveyou.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>And Noah... <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759774.gif' alt=' photo kurtemotionaltwirlinggif.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><u>My thoughts</u><br/>Thief takes us on the tumultuous journey of Caleb and Olivia's everlasting trail of love, jealousy and lies. We get a young C</span>
  <span id="freeText6068290110508988371" style="display:none">This review contains SPOILERS.<br><br>THIS. BOOK.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759767.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mm1neoe5B21s9wbrao1_500_zps454dcd46.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't really know what to say...<br><br>This book was everything I wanted, everything I hated, something that I loved and well as you can see I am a wreck on the emotional scale.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759768.gif" alt=" photo emotionalgif2_zps20f92d89.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><u>The Characters</u><br><br><b>Leah was all</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759769.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mpd8m5Zd0k1qz4rgp_zps40ccfa11.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b>And Olivia was like</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759770.gif" alt=" photo reallybitch.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759771.gif" alt=" photo IdontgiveaF_zps4bbde43c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b>Leah could not accept this...so she was all</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759772.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mpd8knBvHl1qz4rgp_zps5ca70318.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b>Meanwhile Caleb was allll about winning Olivia back</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759773.gif" alt=" photo iloveyou.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>And Noah... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394627ra/759774.gif" alt=" photo kurtemotionaltwirlinggif.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><u>My thoughts</u><br>Thief takes us on the tumultuous journey of Caleb and Olivia's everlasting trail of love, jealousy and lies. We get a young Caleb and his thoughts on his first encounter with Olivia. Along with how their on and off again relationship was seen through his eyes. I must admit some of the things finally shown from his pov is..well..disheartening.<br><br>A LOT of what Olivia may have perceived was misconstrued and it was hard to read through and know how much things could have been different.<br><br>The <b>epilogue</b> was exactly how I thought it should be and I cried the WHOLE time I was reading it. LITERALLY. <br>With everything that happened in this series all I could think about was Karma and her thoughts on this whole ordeal.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394627i/759775.jpg" alt=" photo 4a1c6e34-1d63-403a-81b9-adbdad34b9cf_zps8a77481e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think that is why things may have ended the way it did overall for this couple. And crazy enough I liked it mainly because it was not ideal. And not what I chose it to be. NOPE. Instead it was raw and true to life.<br><br>Wonderful conclusion Ms. Tarryn Fisher!!<br><br><br><b>
  <u>Fave lines said and unsaid</u>
</b><br><br><br><i>
  <b>'Maybe our souls touched underneath that tree. Maybe I decided to love her. Maybe love wasn’t our choice. But when I looked at that woman, I saw myself differently. And it wasn’t in a good light. Not a thing would keep me from her. And that could make a person do things they never thought themselves capable of. What I felt for her scared the hell out of me. It was a consuming obsession.'</b>
</i> -Caleb<br><br><i>
  <b>'The more she rejected me, the more aggressively I fought to tear down her walls.'</b>
</i><br>-Caleb<br><br><i>
  <b>'Olivia is the type of woman that men write songs about. There are about fifty of them on my iPod that make me think of her.'</b>
</i> <br>-Caleb<br><br><i>
  <b>“Why are you forever comparing me to animals and shoes and food?” “Because, I see the world in different shades of Olivia. I’m comparing them to you — not the other way around.”</b>
</i><br>-Olivia and Caleb<br><br><i>
  <b>“Hurts, doesn’t it, motherfucker?”</b>
</i><br>-Cammie<br><br><i>
  <b>“I heard your ex-wife is worst than my first ex-wife.” He smirks. “How did you manage that deal?”<br> “I’m the same type of fool as you, I guess.” He smirks. <br>  “Come over to the house for dinner. Meet my new wife.”</b>
</i><br>-Caleb's bio dad and Caleb<br><br><b>
  <i>“Life does not accommodate you, it shatters you. Love is mean, but it’s good. It keeps us alive. If you need her, then wait. But, right now she’s getting married. It’s her day and you can’t ruin it.”</i>
</b><br>-Luca<br><br><i>
  <b>“I’ve done a lot of things,” she shrugs, trying to play it cool, “you’ll have to be more specific.”   <br>“Olivia.” Her name pings between us, ripping open old wounds and spraying blood across the room. Leah is furious.  <br> “Don’t say that name in my house.”</b>
</i><br>-Leah and Caleb<br><br><br><br>-----------------------------------------------------------------<br><u>Me prior to the book release</u><br>7-21-13 <b>It's OFFICIAL only a matter of time!! Tarryn hit PUBLISH for Thief!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394628ra/759776.gif" alt=" photo fistpump_zps64a10d87.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b>7-19-13 ONE STEP CLOSER TO RELEASE!!! The blurb is up!! WOOOHOOO</b><br><br><i>Note to Self<br>Love is patient; love is kind.<br>Love doesn't boast or brag.<br>There's no arrogance in love;<br>it's never rude, crude, or indecent-it's not self absorbed.<br>Love isn't easily upset.<br>Love doesn't tally wrongs.<br>Love trusts, hopes, and endures no matter what.<br>Love will never become obsolete.<br>I'll fight for her.<br><br>Thief.</i><br><br><b>7-16-13 Straight getting heart palpitations right now....<br>*chants* CALEB IS COMING - CALEB IS COMING - CALEB IS COMING!!! <br>GET R E A D Y! Tarryn posted on Facebook for everyone to do their re-reads now!!!! You know what that means!!!! <i>CALEB IS COMING!!!! SOON!!!!!</i></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394628ra/759777.gif" alt=" photo yesss_zpsbbfa0b82.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b> KICKING-SCREAMING-SHOUTING<br>I CAN'T WAIT FOR THIS BOOK!!!!!!!!</b><br><br><b>UPDATE 2/20/2013</b> WHOA! Just saw the cover... HOT DAMN...<br><br><a href="http://s1308.beta.photobucket.com/user/aim4fashion/media/Final%20Edited%20version%20used%20for%20book%20reviews/e8048d23-dad4-49d6-a8df-b5777e97879b_zpsbfff63b9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_436225451" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/436225451" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/436225451?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer436225451" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15370836376128923354">♦ ♦ <b>Warning</b>: While there are no intentional spoilers, there may be some things that may give something away. I try to be ambiguous but still. Stop reading reviews and trust me...just read the book! ♦ ♦<br/><br/>We finally get Caleb's POV and for those of us waiting...anxiously, you just don't know how good that is. There have been sooo many questions and sooo many theories on why Caleb did certain things and how he felt...it was just a big sigh of relief to get those answers. <br/><br/>This is the third and final b</span>
  <span id="freeText15370836376128923354" style="display:none">♦ ♦ <b>Warning</b>: While there are no intentional spoilers, there may be some things that may give something away. I try to be ambiguous but still. Stop reading reviews and trust me...just read the book! ♦ ♦<br><br>We finally get Caleb's POV and for those of us waiting...anxiously, you just don't know how good that is. There have been sooo many questions and sooo many theories on why Caleb did certain things and how he felt...it was just a big sigh of relief to get those answers. <br><br>This is the third and final book of the Love Me With Lies series and I loved it. It was almost as good as the first book. If you don't know by now, Tarryn Fisher loves to make things messy and she especially messes with your mind. I have never read a book again right after I read it the first time but I did with the first book of this series. And yes...it's that good and it's that different. Another thing she did is write the second book from the villain's POV. Obviously, most people didn't really care for that but there were all kinds of juicy nuggets in that story. You won't want to skip it. <br><br>Back to Caleb...Caleb, Caleb, Caleb, it was sooo AMAZEBALLS!! People...this is the way to write a story!! Okay, maybe I'm not a big fan of the past and present chapters and I would LOVE the whole series written in chronological order with everyone's POV but...I'll take what I get. And what I got was a wonderful LOVE story. A story that's a little bit dirty, a little bit messy and a whole LOT real. <br><br>Tarryn Fisher did not miss a beat. She gave us the answers to every single question and set us straight with every single theory. I was really nervous that she would throw some whammies in there but for the most part, I was really happy with how things went. Of course, there are some things I'm not happy with but that's life. <br><br>Peter Pan...Caleb I didn't think I could love you as much as I did in the beginning but I'm sooo happy you proved me wrong. I LOVED getting in your head. It was great seeing you work your way through your feelings for Olivia and <i>accepting</i> them. And I loved that you fought...and you fought well...even though there were some snags, I liked how things worked out in the end. <br><br>Speaking of Peter Pan...I LOVED that! Just another thing to add to the list of the tree, the orange grove, Cherry Garcia, the penny, Airport Blue, the basketball, the shot, gardenias, Duchess, the house in Naples, THE RING!, sugar cubes, backward names, the color Red, llamas and penguins, heart orgasms, uppercut hugs, breakfrast, Coldplay, Great Expectations, the boat, pinky holding, lavender blankets, Cheeto dust and OMG matching ugly t-shirts. I LOVE how TF adds these little sweet things into the story. It makes it so much more relatable and <i>real</i>. <br><br>Olivia...I wished she would've come around sooner BUT...I'm impressed with how she handled herself. I loved that we got a chapter of her POV because I really missed her. I hated what happened in the end though but again, I'm glad things worked out (for the most part). <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/624798.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The sex scenes are steamy but they are not detailed. This story is more about the feelings and the emotions...the sex is just bonus. And hell ya to the EVERY DAY!!<br><br>Leah...still a b*tch and even bigger one if that's possible. I was really sad about it...I really thought she was coming around. Oh well...'nuff said. <br><br>Noah...Wow, so didn't see that one coming but I love TF's ingenuity in figuring something out that worked. I was a bit shocked to not like Noah anymore especially since he was such a great guy. I understand his reasons though and you just knew it would have to be something intense. <br><br>Cammie...oh Cammie, what a wonderful best friend even though she may have caused things to wait longer, I really think she thought she was taking care of Olivia and she really had the best intentions. And I loved how Caleb knew them sooo well. Gremlins...LOL! <br><br>Steve...I LOVE him...who knew? but oh sooo sad! <br><br>And finally Estella...torture, Tarryn Fisher, torture!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/624799.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The feels...ugh...I love and hate that it feels sooo good! I loved the Twilight part of "One Month Gone" "Two Months Gone" "Three Months" "Four"...that was a killer but bravo! <br><br>Everyone thinks Caleb is the Thief but I really feel like time was the thief...ten years. It still kills me. <br><br>And the epilogue...another love/hate relationship. ~sigh~ <br><br>I'm sad that it's over and maybe one day I will read the whole series over back to back...or just maybe The Opportunist and The Thief. Yeah...maybe just that. <br><br>Definitely looking forward to what else Tarryn Fisher comes up with. Whatever it is, I know it will be something new and refreshing and it will definitely mess with your mind! <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/623922.gif" width="400" height="030" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Favorite quotes:<br><br>♦ <i>(OMG...how can I limit myself? I think I almost highlighted the whole book so bear with me or feel free to skip them because I'm sure there will be a lot...(Yes, there are!) and there may possibly be spoilers (Yes, there is)!!</i> ♦ <br><br>♥ " She’s mine. She always has been, she always will be."<br><br>♥ <i>"Can anyone be more beautiful than Olivia?"</i><br><br>♥ "But when I looked at that woman, I saw myself differently. And it wasn’t in a good light. Not a thing would keep me from her. And that could make a person do things they never thought themselves capable of. What I felt for her scared the hell out of me. It was a consuming obsession."<br><br>♥ "My heart is still broken. I’m trying to figure out how to live without what I really want."<br><br>♥ "Selfish, self-centered Caleb Drake loved a girl so much he could already feel himself changing to accommodate her needs. <br><br>I fell. <br>Hard. <br><br>For the rest of this life and probably the next. <br><br>I wanted her — every last inch of her stubborn, combative, catty heart."<br><br>♦ “It’s his massive penis, isn’t it? He could just smack Dobson with it and he’d-”<br><br><i>(see...gotta love Cammie!)</i><br><br>♦ "Don't you wish Dobson loved Leah instead?" <br><br><i>(another Cammie nugget!)</i><br><br>♥ “Did you really just call me Peter Pan?”<br><br>“I’ve called you worse.” I eased the car into the traffic. <br><br>“A llama,” she said. “I loved that.”<br><br>♥ “You know,” I say, leaning across the table and taking her hand. “I could have sex with a thousand women, and it wouldn’t feel like it did that night in the orange grove.”<br><br>♥ "I don't love anything more than I love you."<br><br>♥ “Let me carry you out. I’ll never let you touch the ground. I was made to carry you, Olivia. You’re fucking heavy with all of your guilt and self-loathing. But, I can do it. Because I love you.” <br><br>♥ “Yeah, you got married, didn’t you? But, you only did it because you thought we were over — and we’re not over. We’ll never be over. If you think that little piece of metal on your finger can shield off your feelings for me, you’re wrong. I wore one for five years and there wasn’t a day that went by where I wasn’t wishing it were you.” <br><br>♥ Steve shook his head. “Some people take more work than others. You fell in love with a really complicated woman. You can weigh how hard things can and will be for the two of you, but what you really need to consider is if you can live without her.”<br><br><i>(Steve is sooo smart!)</i><br><br>♥ “When I’m with you, every emotion I can possibly feel comes spilling out. I drown in them. I want to run to you, and I want to run away.”<br><br>♥ “I want to go on anniversary dinners with you, I want to wrap Christmas presents with you. I want to fight with you about stupid things and then hold you down in my bed and make it up to you. I want to have more cake batter fights and camping trips. I want your future, Olivia. Please come back to me.”<br><br>♥ “Why don’t you blush? No matter what I say — you never blush.” <br><br>She smirks. “Because, I’m a f*cking bad*ss.” <br><br>“Yeah, you are,” I say softly. I kiss the tip of her nose.<br><br>♦ “What if she doesn’t choose me?” <br><br>He grins and leans forward in his seat. “Well, there’s always Leah…” <br><br>My laugh starts in my chest and works its way out. <br><br>“Worst joke ever, Steve … worst joke ever.”<br><br>♥ “I’m fine,” she says firmly. <br><br>I grab her wrist and pull her into a hug, kissing the top of her head. “No, you’re not. I’m your soulmate. I’m the only one who knows how to heal you.”<br><br>♥ “How is it that you always let me go so easily then? Why don’t you know that I want you to fight for me?” <br><br><i>(the million dollar question...)</i><br><br>♥ “Because, I see the world in different shades of Olivia. I’m comparing them to you — not the other way around.” <br><br>“Wow,” she says, taking a sip of her wine. “You’ve got it bad.”<br><br>♥ “This is the last time I’m going to say this, so listen carefully.” I can smell her skin. “You and I are happening. No one is keeping us apart again. Not Noah or Cammie, and least of all, f*cking Leah. You are mine. Do you understand me?”<br><br>♥ “Olivia, I once told you that I would love again, and that you would hurt forever. Do you remember?” <br><br>She nods. It’s a painful memory for both of us. <br><br>“It was a lie. I knew it was a lie, even as I said it. I’ve never loved anyone after you. I never will.”<br><br>♥ "You couldn’t get rid of the past. You couldn’t ignore it, or bury it, or throw it over the balcony. You just had to learn to live beside it. It had to peacefully co-exist with your present. If I could figure out how to do that, I could be okay. I took the penny inside and pulled my copy of <i>Great Expectations</i> off the bookshelf. I taped the penny to the title page and slid the book back in. There. Right where it belonged." <br><br>♦ “You’re a criminal,” Olivia says. “And you’re actually looking kind of chubby.”<br><br><i>(Way to tell her, Olivia!)</i><br><br>♥ “If I make this shot, will you go out with me?” I hold my cup like it’s a basketball and look from her to the trashcan. <br><br>“Yeah,” she says, smiling. “Yeah, I will.” <br><br>I make the shot. <br><br>♥ She wiggles and I know what she wants. <br><br>“Again?” I suck on one of her fingers and she shivers. <br><br>“Again,” she says. “And again, and again, and again…”<br><br>♥ “I’ll do whatever I have to do to protect you. I’ll lie, cheat, and steal to make you okay. I’ll share your suffering, and I’ll carry you when you’re weighed down. I’ll never leave you, not even when you ask me to. Do you believe me?” <br><br>She touches my face with the tips of her fingers and nods. <br><br>“You’re strong enough to protect your heart and mine, and your heart from mine. I’ll give you everything I have because from the day I met you, it’s belonged to you.”<br><br>♥ "She is the only woman I’ve seen that gets more beautiful with age. She is the only woman I see."<br><br><i>(That's it!! Don't say I didn't warn you!)</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="15370836376128923354" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_482894723" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/482894723" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/482894723?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=emotional-rollercoaster">emotional-rollercoaster</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer482894723" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13200443744080842069"><b>
  <blockquote>♥♥♥ 5 STARS!!!! ♥♥♥</blockquote>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401649i/779816._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/> <b><i>Thief</i> was easily my most anticipated book of 2013. All year I've been waiting for this third and final part of the <i>Love Me With Lies-</i>series, and I can honestly say it was 100% worth the wait!</b> <br/><br/>While <i>The Opportunist</i> was told from Olivia's POV, and <i>Dirty Red</i> was told from Leah's side, we now finally get Caleb's side of the story. We finally find out what went through his head during all of the important events of the two previous books and we find out how he reacts after the</span>
  <span id="freeText13200443744080842069" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>♥♥♥ 5 STARS!!!! ♥♥♥</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401649i/779816._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b><i>Thief</i> was easily my most anticipated book of 2013. All year I've been waiting for this third and final part of the <i>Love Me With Lies-</i>series, and I can honestly say it was 100% worth the wait!</b> <br><br>While <i>The Opportunist</i> was told from Olivia's POV, and <i>Dirty Red</i> was told from Leah's side, we now finally get Caleb's side of the story. We finally find out what went through his head during all of the important events of the two previous books and we find out how he reacts after the bomb Leah dropped on him at the end of Dirty Red. At the beginning of the story, I had so many unanswered questions but by the end of the book, all my questions were answered.<br><br><br>♦ Although there are many players in this story, in the end, it's all about the two major ones, <b>Caleb Drake</b> and <b>Olivia Kaspen</b>. ♦<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Olivia. I've lost her three times. The first was to impatience. The second was to a lie so dense we couldn't work our way through it. And the third time - this time - I've lost her to Noah."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401649i/779817._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Caleb has been infatuated with Olivia since the moment they first met. When you think about it, it's actualy crazy that two people who were so in love and so perfect for each other, still managed to destroy everything they have. Most of it, all because of lies. But, deep down, they've always known their connection is too strong to ignore.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"She's mine. She always has been, always will be."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>They have so much history that I couldn't help but root the entire time I was reading this series, that they would eventually <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[get their HEA <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, just because they seem so perfect for each other. But things in life aren't always that simple, and the emotional and heartbreaking parts in this story are the exact proof of that fact.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401649i/779818._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"She has the kind of love that can stain your soul, make you beg not to have one, just to escape the spell she's put you under. I've tried to break myself from her over and over, but it's pointless. I've got more of her in my veins than blood."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>What I loved about reading Caleb's POV in Thief is that it's obvious how much he always has and always will love Olivia. There were times during The Opportunist and Dirty where I doubted his sincerity and his choice of action. At times, I was even infuriated with the way he acted, but now, because of his determination to win Olivia back, even though the chances are he might not succeed, I've really started to love him again.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401649i/779819.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Lies, it sounds demented to want a woman's lies. But Olivia loves you with her lies. She lies about how she's feeling, how she's hurting, how she wants you when she tells you she doesn't. She lies to protect you and herself."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Olivia is so damaged by her past that lying is the only way she knows how to cope. She seems cold and composed on the outside, but throughout the story, Caleb manages to break through her icy exterior and he manages to make her realize she still has feelings for him even though she's married to Noah. The only question is whether she'll continue to aknowledge those feelings or whether she'll continue to lie about them, even to herself.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401649i/779820._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their story is filled with anguish and heartbreak and there were sooo many times that I felt like pulling my hair out. I wanted to yell at the characters to *finally* make the right decision and to follow their heart. At times I hated Caleb and Olivia, other times I loved them (Leah, on the other hand, I hated ALL the time!). They are not conventional or very easy to relate to- characters. They lie, cheat and deceive to get what they want. But in the end, and because of the way Tarryn Fisher told their story, they managed to capture my heart and all I wanted was for them to finally find peace and happiness <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[preferably with each other! ;-) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Let me carry you out. I'll never let you touch the ground. I was made to carry you, Olivia. You're fucking heavy with all of your guilt and self loathing. But, I can do it. Because I love you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401649i/779821._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br>All in all, this series is an absolute <b>MUST READ</b>. I've never read anything like it and I don't think I'll ever come across anything like it ever again. It was an amazing, unforgettable, brilliant series that will forever remain on my all time favorites shelf. The many parts I highlighted throughout the story indicate what an exceptionally talented writer Tarryn Fisher is and I can't wait to read more of her work in the future! I will for sure read whatever it is she writes next. ;-)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401649i/779822.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
<b><i>"Broken people give broken love. And we are all a little broken. You just have to forgive and sew up the wounds love delivers, and move on."</i></b><br><br>♥♥♥</blockquote></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="13200443744080842069" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer487177404" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17362164360908845194"><b>
  <i>”Maybe this is finally our time. Maybe.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402287i/781789._SX540_.jpg' width='401' height='375' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>After reading <i>Dirty Red</i>, I religiously stalked Tarryn Fischer’s Face Book status’ regarding her process in writing the <i>Thief</i>. When Tarryn hit the publish button I actually froze. Weirdly, my fear had me terrified to start if you can you believe it? I was so damn invested in Olivia and Caleb and what awaited me in these 234 pages that the conclusion both excited and terrified me…I kid you not!<br/><br/><br/>Tarryn’s writing is PURE BRILLIANCE!! Caleb’s pov was ABSOLUT</span>
  <span id="freeText17362164360908845194" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>”Maybe this is finally our time. Maybe.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402287i/781789._SX540_.jpg" width="401" height="375" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>After reading <i>Dirty Red</i>, I religiously stalked Tarryn Fischer’s Face Book status’ regarding her process in writing the <i>Thief</i>. When Tarryn hit the publish button I actually froze. Weirdly, my fear had me terrified to start if you can you believe it? I was so damn invested in Olivia and Caleb and what awaited me in these 234 pages that the conclusion both excited and terrified me…I kid you not!<br><br><br>Tarryn’s writing is PURE BRILLIANCE!! Caleb’s pov was ABSOLUTE PERFECTION. My heart pounded the entire read as the stomach churned till the very last page.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>”“Lies, it sounds demented to want a woman’s lies. But, Olivia loves you with her lies. She lies about how she’s feeling, how she’s hurting, how she wants you when she tells you she doesn’t. She lies to protect you and herself.”</i>
</b><br><br><br>Caleb Drake is divorced and will stop at nothing this time around for a future with Olivia. <br><br><br>The story sways from past and present shining a light on past events while the present gives slivers of hope and then snatches it away then gives hope back again. All the while I pictured Tarryn chuckling at her readers’ reactions. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>”Eventually.” She sighs. “That word is so us, isn’t it? Eventually, you’ll tell me you’re faking amnesia. Eventually, I’ll tell you that I’m pretending not to know you. Eventually, we’ll come back together, fall apart, come back together.”</i>
</b><br><br><br>Questions that have stumped readers are finally put to rest and answered. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>”She only wanted to see the bad. Maybe it was for the best. Maybe all I saw was my love and I hadn’t weighed the consequences of that love.”</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>”Olivia and I never had a chance. The whole time we were destroying ourselves, someone else was having a go at it too.”</i>
</b><br><br><br>The present brings Caleb and Olivia once again in and out of each other lives. All the while neither one is ever really ready to fully break their connection. Quite possibly their connection is unbreakable through all the lies, deceit, heartache and unsaid words. A reader pulls for happiness for both characters while afraid to dream of a hea. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402287i/781790._SX540_.jpg" width="401" height="375" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><br><i>Thief</i> is an intense, heart pounding, unforgettable conclusion to a timeless series of imperfect love. This couple will forever hold a special place in my heart. <br><br><b>
  <i>”I don’t love anything more than I love you.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"The sum of all the things we shouldn't have done in our lives is enough to kill us with the weight, Caleb Drake. Neither you, nor I, nor anyone else in this life could possibly know the chain reaction our decisions cause. If you're to blame, then so am I." </i>
</b><br></span>
