<div id="review_688145806" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/688145806" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/688145806?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=pregnant-heroines">pregnant-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer688145806" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1961642951495319047">In this third book in the series, we finally get to hear Caleb's side of the story. I have been continually amazed by this author's ability to retell the same story over and over, albeit from a different vantage point, and keep it feeling fresh and new. Just like in the previous books, 'Thief' is divided into past and present timeframes, with the present portions revealing new events as they transpire. <br/><br/>After reading 'Dirty Red', I was especially interested to see how Caleb could've loved a woman</span>
  <span id="freeText1961642951495319047" style="display:none">In this third book in the series, we finally get to hear Caleb's side of the story. I have been continually amazed by this author's ability to retell the same story over and over, albeit from a different vantage point, and keep it feeling fresh and new. Just like in the previous books, 'Thief' is divided into past and present timeframes, with the present portions revealing new events as they transpire. <br /><br />After reading 'Dirty Red', I was especially interested to see how Caleb could've loved a woman like Leah. The truth was surprising. I had to reevaluate my feelings for Caleb as new information was brought to light. Leah's underhanded, manipulative ways continued to blow my mind, as even more of her tactics were exposed in this book.<br /><br />I was glad to have confirmation that Caleb actually loved Olivia as much as she loved him. The earlier books left me feeling uncertain of the depth of his feelings. Part of me was afraid to read this, worried I'd find out that he had just played both women for years. Thankfully, that wasn't the case.<br /><br />Although I continued to be frustrated with the ease with which Caleb seemed to walk away from Olivia, I now understand where he was coming from. Ultimately, he came to regret his repeated failure to fight for her. <br /><br />Overall, I was happy with how this story ended. Caleb and Olivia finally got some happiness, after years of disaster and tragedy. Nothing had ever come easily for these two, so it's fitting that they didn't have a unicorns and rainbows type of conclusion. I loved every minute of this series!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1961642951495319047" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_858292724" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/858292724" />
    <a title="Shell The Belle " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15880350-shell-the-belle"><img alt="Shell The Belle " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1399759491p2/15880350.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/858292724?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shell The Belle " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shell The Belle " href="/user/show/15880350-shell-the-belle">Shell The Belle </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer858292724" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9897344872901908028"><b>*Slight Edit*</b><br/><br/><b>One Very Disappointed And Not At All convinced Star</b><br/><br/><b>*CONTAINS LOTS OF SPOILERS – SPOILERS EVERYWHERE*</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>*Contains spoilers and should not be read until you have read all three books, if that is what you are planning to do*</i>
</b> – or read this review first, and maybe I can save the wasted time of reading the books to begin with. You have been warned – about the spoilers, that is!<br/><br/>I know most of my friends who have read this book have loved it, but I really hated it. Or more so, I hated the</span>
  <span id="freeText9897344872901908028" style="display:none"><b>*Slight Edit*</b><br><br><b>One Very Disappointed And Not At All convinced Star</b><br><br><b>*CONTAINS LOTS OF SPOILERS – SPOILERS EVERYWHERE*</b><br><br><b>
  <i>*Contains spoilers and should not be read until you have read all three books, if that is what you are planning to do*</i>
</b> – or read this review first, and maybe I can save the wasted time of reading the books to begin with. You have been warned – about the spoilers, that is!<br><br>I know most of my friends who have read this book have loved it, but I really hated it. Or more so, I hated the characters. Caleb and Olivia are horrible people who both do horrible things to other people, and I just don’t get why so many people like them. Others talk disparagingly about Leah, but I don’t see why she is seen as so much the bad guy, all she did was try damn hard to keep her man, who she truly believed loved her and whom she loved. Olivia and Caleb, on the other hand, have both done some despicable things. Olivia being the worst. <br><br>Anyway, I am going to re-title this book, and it is going to be called:<br><br><b>
  <u>The Convenient Book Of Convenient Conveniences And Even More Convenient Coincidences</u>
</b><br><br>I have no idea why it is called Thief, it doesn’t represent anything really.<br><br>Seriously, it was all about how the Author could make the story right after the first two books – hardly anything gelled with the previous two books.<br><br>In <b>The Opportunist,</b> I knew by the end of that book that I didn’t like either of the MCs. Neither of them seemed to have any redeemable features or qualities; they were both callous calculating nasty individuals who really didn’t give a flying monkeys vajayjay about who they hurt in life, so long as they either got their own way or got revenge. I <b>hated</b> them both. <br><br>Book two, Dirty Red, was a strange one as it was told from Caleb’s other girlfriend/wife’s POV. It was actually refreshing and I really enjoyed that book and the main character Leah. Yea, she was a liar, but hell she was in good company with Caleb and Olivia huh?<br><br>Book three, this book, is from Caleb’s POV. It starts where Dirty Red finished. Again it is told in past/present/past/present chapters the same as the other two books were. <br><br>Well, lets start with the beginning of the book. At the end of Book Two, Leah, in a fit of pique, having been devastated, wrecked and ruined by Caleb and his confessions of never loving her, always hankering after Olivia, and even faking the amnesia (I will deal with <b>
  <i>that</i>
</b> little gem further down – don’t worry, I <b>will</b> get to it) so Leah is on the floor, a shattered, broken and shredded mess, reeling from this, she then stands and tells him that Estella, their daughter, isn’t his. Well, that’s one way to hurt a guy and give him a gut wrench. <br><br>So, what does Caleb do? Demand a DNA test? Which would be no problem for even him to arrange – he <b>is</b> listed as the baby’s father so he could just scoop her (the baby) up there and then and take her with him to get one. Of course, yes, because that is what a doting father (which Caleb is, btw) who loved his daughter more than anything <i>
  <b>would do</b>
</i> right? Right???<br><br><b>Except he doesn’t.</b><br><br>He just takes Leah’s word for it, knowing <b>
  <u>KNOWING</u>
</b> what a lying evil bitch she can be. How very, what’s the word here? Oh yes, <i>
  <b>convenient.</b>
</i><br><br>Again there was so much <i>telling</i> instead of <i>showing</i> in this book just like there was in book one. I lost count of the numerous times Olivia was referred to as a “badass” but nothing, and I mean <i>nothing</i> made me think that about her in any way. The only thing she did was near the end when she slapped Leah across the face twice – a scene where the Author had <u>conveniently</u> reverted Leah back to how she was in book one and the beginning of book two.<br><br>We also had Caleb <i>telling</i> us over and over how sexy and gorgeous Olivia was and the effect she had on men, and AGAIN I’m thinking “really? Fucking really??” Where? How? SHOW ME FFS!<br><br><u>Examples</u><br><br><b>Caleb:</b> <i>”Olivia burned. When she walked into a room you could feel her fire. It rolled off of her in waves. She was angry and passionate and fearless”</i> <br><br>But as the reader I didn’t see this! There was never any description of <i>how</i> she did this. <br><br>Another scene at half way through the book in a club, where Caleb sees Olivia dancing; <br><br><br><i>”As she (Olivia) dances, she lifts her arms above her head and sways side to side. Then she climbs onto a speaker. A guy is climbing on it too. Everyone is watching. Olivia’s friend shouts something at her, and she bends down to hear her. Her dress gapes and I see cleavage. I get her down from the speaker and hold her against me so she can get the full effect of what I am about to say. “Do you feel that? (his erection btw) That’s what you’ve done to every guy in this room with your dancing”</i><br><br>Again, this is not shown in the writing; we are not shown how all the other guys in the vicinity are affected by her, we only have Caleb’s <i>say so</i> on it. <br>But then he goes on like this;<br><br> <i>“I can see the effect my words have on her. She doesn’t like to be the subject of sexual fantasy – little prude.”</i><br><br><b>WHAT??? Dancing seductively, climbing onto a speaker in the club, showing everyone her cleavage on full beam, and <i>she doesn’t want to be the subject of sexual fantasy???</i> Get real. </b><br><br><b>DO YOU THINK YOUR READERS ARE STUPID OR WHAT?</b><br><br><br>I said in my reviews of <b>The Opportunist</b> and <b>Dirty Red</b> that I saw real brilliance in Tarryn Fisher’s writing. But this, <b>Thief</b> is almost like it wasn’t written by the same Author <i>at all</i>. <br><br>There were huge inconsistencies in the story timeline. Almost as though the Author had gotten mixed up herself;<br><br>For example, at one point Olivia is crying, talking to Caleb about her miscarriage, but she doesn’t <i>actually</i> tell him about the said miscarriage until the next (present) chapter??<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=dom2v5" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398778637ra/9462225.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> I wonder if Tarryn Fisher was on a tight deadline and just had to finish this as quickly as she could, because I swear, <i>I swear</i> it was as though who ever wrote this was just making it up as they went along, and kept changing their mind about certain things but didn’t have time to re-write it so just made up shit to fit.<br><br>Take for example the situation with the child, Estella; first she wasn’t Caleb’s (cos Leah said so remember?) Then Leah says she IS Calebs. Then she isn’t again, because he has (at bloody last!!) a paternity test that says he <i>
  <b>is not the biological father of the child</b>
</i>. So there we have it. <br><br>Wait for it.<br><br>Then <i>
  <b>she <u>IS</u> his again and he IS the Father because hey bloody presto the fucking paternity test was WRONG!! </b>
</i><br><br>Yea, like that happens a lot. All you scum from off of Jeremy Kyle whose DNA results told you that you were the Daddy, rest easy! <br><br>Yea, I know it probably happens in a very tiny percentage of tests, but feck me if this wasn’t just the slightest bit <i>
  <b>
    <u>convenient.</u>
  </b>
</i> Again.<br><br><b>
  <u>About The Story Itself.</u>
</b><br><br>The whole debacle of Olivia and Caleb’s relationship was exhausting and infuriating. Again I seriously <i>don't</i> get why so many people were rooting for them. All they did was go around and about for over ten fucking years messing up other people’s lives in the process. <br><br>From the very beginning of their relationship, back in College, there were signs that neither of them was really invested in each other that much. I understand the chase and all that at their first couple of meetings, but when, after what seemed like a lovely first date, This happens;<br><br><b>Olivia</b> “I just don’t think we’re compatible”<br><b>Caleb</b> “That’s not how it feels to me”<br> "Um, well I'm sorry. I guess we are just on two different wavelengths”<br><b>Caleb</b> "I know you like me as much as I like you, but it’s your choice, and I am a gentleman. You want me to back off? Okay. Goodbye, Olivia”<br><br><b>Caleb</b> I knew I should fight her on this, but the last thing I wanted to do was chase after someone who didn’t want me, or didn’t know they did.<br><br>You see I just don’t get it, if he loved her as much as we are TOLD he does, HE WOULD NOT WALK AWAY!<br><br>A few paragraphs later and he tells us he has <b>"moved on"</b>. He meets Jessica, (remember Jessica Alexander - whose life Olivia all but ruined by talking her into an abortion because she knew Caleb would be furious about it, and then made sure not only he found out but the whole college?) Caleb says this about Jessica;<br><br><i><b>“She was sexy and kind and ditzy – my type exactly. She took away the constant edge I felt and Olivia gradually receded to the back of my mind. I could even joke about it after a while and it seemed funny now that I had become obsessed with Olivia when I barley knew her. Everything was going my way. I wanted to marry Jessica”</b></i><br><br>Of course, that is when Olivia decided <i>she</i> wanted Caleb, and plotted to get him back. <br><br>This goes on and on throughout the whole book. <br><br><b>Neither of them wants the other until they cant have them.</b><br><br>Rinse and repeat.<br><br>And we supposedly learn what really happened with the Caleb cheating incident in the first book – you know where Olivia walks in on him with someone in his office and it finishes their relationship? Well guess what?? <b>Turns out, Caleb wasn’t actually and didn’t actually <i>cheat</i> at all.</b><br><br><b>That’s right, folks, it <u><i>conveniently</i></u> turns out that he was just <i>comforting</i> said girl on his desk, and was in fact telling her how he was going to propose to Olivia that weekend!!<br><br>WHAT.THE.ACTUAL.FUCK?</b><br><br>Are we the readers just supposed to swallow this?? <br><br>Go back and read Olivia’s version in the first book, then read Caleb’s version. Doesn’t stack up right? Well, after all, they <i>are</i> both liars, so it’s really anybody’s guess what really happened. <br><br>But it’s all very convenient, anyway.<br><br>When we found out in book one that Caleb had faked his amnesia, I didnt think it was av<i>romantic</i> gesture at all - I just thought he was a fucking coward who was too spineless to tell Leah the truth and just man the fuck up and go after what he really wanted. <br><br>Time goes back to the present, and I don’t get why she turns up at Caleb’s flat after she gets Dobson off either. She hasn’t seen him since Rome. Why just turn up there?? And as for inviting him to dinner with her and Noah, saying Noah has always wanted to meet him? Nope. Don’t get that either. <br>And when he does go for dinner, his date he brings along is none other than Jessica Alexander. Having met up with her again three months earlier, he says this about her;<br><br><i><b>”I really like her. I <u>loved</u> her once.”</b></i><br><br>Do you know Caleb; here is one piece of advice from Johnny Depp;<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2s0g7c3" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398778637i/9462226.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Whilst at Olivia's condo having this evening get together with each other and respective partners, Caleb makes the following observations:<br><br><i><b>"It looks different to the last time I was here. It looks like a home".</b></i><br><br>That’s cos it is, Olivia and Noah’s home you idiot!!<br><br>And<br><br><i><b>”I see genuine affection in her eyes when she looks at Noah. Her ever cold eyes travel between the two of us. Choose me. Her gaze lands on Noah. Their intimacy makes me jealous. Rageful.”</b></i><br><br>He even says how “there is still fun to be had” and I got the impression it was all a game to him, despite that fact that other people, Jessica and Noah to name but two, are going to get truly hurt if they don’t stop their silly games. <br><br>This is the texting between them the next day:<br><br><b>Olivia</b> – <i>"Well?”</i><br><b>Caleb</b> - <i>Well what”</i><br><b>Olivia</b> - <i>”Fuck you. Don’t play games. What did you think of Noah?”</i><br><b>Caleb</b> - <i>"Nice. What did you think of Jessica?”</i><br><b>Olivia</b> - <i>”Same stupid slut. Don’t fall in love with her”</i><br><br>And that’s it for another fucking year! They don’t see or hear of each other, <b>because, you know, they love each other so much and cant bear to be apart</b> – yea, doesn’t make sense to me either.<br><br>After said year, during which Caleb and Jessica have all but moved in together, getting on really well, fucking Olivia calls him out of the blue because some psycho she put away last year has escaped and she is scared! And like the cuntfish that he is, he leaves his bed with Jessica in it and runs to help the poor little cow, disappearing with her for three days till the said psycho is caught again. Then he finally breaks up with Jessica for good.<br><br>Still Caleb and Olivia don’t get together, they go round and round and we learn about why she isn’t entirely happy with Noah. His sister has cystic fibrosis and he doesn’t want children because he carries the gene. <br><br>Eventually after a load more crap they <b>DO</b> eventually end up together, after ruining Jessica, Noah and Leah’s lives. <br><br>Here is what I wish for Caleb and Olivia;<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=28lszus" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399556180i/9566644.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>For the life of me, I just didn’t know where the author was going with any of this. So many things were just – wrong. Don’t get me started on the stupid storyline of Leah not leaving a contact number when Estella went to England to stay with Caleb and she went away with her boyfriend. Poor little Estella had a really bad car accident (it is really bad, I didn't like that) and of course they <u><b>Conveniently</b></u> couldn’t contact Leah for days, making her out to be the atypical bad Mom again. <br><br><b>NOPE. NOT BUYING THAT CRAP.</b><br><br>And what was with <i><b>THAT.FUCKING.EPILOGUE.</b></i><br><br>After all the running around, all the nonsense, all the rinse and repeat, they do end up together but, they never marry? Huh? Marriage is so important to both of them we were constantly told!!<br><br>Anyway, they never do have a baby together, Olivia cant carry them to term it seems. So much for the child issue being the only reason she divorced Noah. And then, AND THEN, Olivia gets cancer?? <br><br>Please, if you are going to write a sentimental story based on kind of real life stuff, do it, and do it properly, but don’t try to combine them into a piece of NA romance like this, the two JUST DO NOT FIT. It’s a despicable thing to do to your reader. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2lwoex5" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398778637ra/9462227.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Estella, the child, ended up living with Caleb from the age of nine. What? No way would that happen!! <i><b>Convenient much.</b></i> <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=dbkxkx" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398778637ra/9462228.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Caleb says, “Fortunately, Estella is nothing like her mother.” Well, all I can say Caleb is let’s hope she’s not a stupid lying cheating selfish prick like you, then, huh! <br><br>I would love to know what happened to Leah - obviously TF didn't have time to tell us more about her - who did she end up marrying?? I hope it was Seth. I would so love to see a sequel to Dirty Red, in Leah's voice again, and in the same brilliant writing style that Dirty Red was written in.<br><br>All in all, I will never understand why this book has so many high ratings; I am, once again, in the minority of those that - <br><br><i><b>JUST DIDN’T GET IT.</b></i><br><br>One more thing – what was that whole thing with Caleb saying everybody’s name backwards in his head?? I was halfway through before I realised what the hell he was doing!!!<br><br><b><i>You can read my reviews of The Opportunist and Dirty Red here;</i></b> <br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/830066379?book_show_action=false">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/845818816?book_show_action=false">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="9897344872901908028" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2607684-megan-reading-books-like-a-boss-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer467596353" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9446222985230244151"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383830356i/6679182._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Check out this AMAZING trailer made by The Book Avenue here: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?feature=player_embedded&v=4dORIZnrvgM'>http://www.youtube.com/watch?feature=...</a></b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <p>
    <em>
      <strong>“Life does not accommodate you, it shatters you. Love is mean, but it’s good. It keeps us alive.” </strong>
    </em>
  </p>
</blockquote><br/>I have agonized and stressed over how in the world I was going to review this book - this wonderful beautiful book. <em>Thief</em> is the final book of the Love Me With Lies series, an achingly poignant series that touched me so deeply. These characters have embedded their way into my </span>
  <span id="freeText9446222985230244151" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383830356i/6679182._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Check out this AMAZING trailer made by The Book Avenue here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?feature=player_embedded&amp;v=4dORIZnrvgM">http://www.youtube.com/watch?feature=...</a></b><br><br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <em>
      <strong>“Life does not accommodate you, it shatters you. Love is mean, but it’s good. It keeps us alive.” </strong>
    </em>
  </p>
</blockquote><br>I have agonized and stressed over how in the world I was going to review this book - this wonderful beautiful book. <em>Thief</em> is the final book of the Love Me With Lies series, an achingly poignant series that touched me so deeply. These characters have embedded their way into my heart. Caleb and Olivia are in me so deep that I there is no way I will ever forget them.<br><br><em>Thief</em> was everything I was hoping for, but nothing what I expected. I had all these crazy theories floating around in my head, few of which actually came true (thank God). Leave it to Tarryn Fisher to make to take all of my expectations and throw them out the proverbial window. This series is a testament to Fisher's writing talent and staying power in the book world. Fisher is able to make her readers truly feel connected to these fictional characters. I know I am not alone when I wonder where they are now. I wonder what they're doing at this very moment. Not many books make me feel so rooted in their fictional lives. It makes me feel a little crazy.<br><br>Like <em>Dirty Red</em>, <em>Thief</em> started out with a bang. Caleb is sitting in his condo (yes, the same condo he had during he and Olivia's relationship) watching Olivia win Dobson's murder trial. He and Leah have been divorced for a period of time at this point. Even watching Olivia on the television he is transfixed and finds everything she does beautiful and enrapturing. His love for her is so deep and so raw even after all these years.<br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <em>
      <strong>"Olivia is a piece of art. You have to know how to interpret her, how to see the beauty under the harsh lines of her personality...She has the kind of love that can stain your soul, make you beg not to have one, just to escape the spell she's put you under. I"ve tried to break myself of her over and over, but it's pointless. I've got more of her in my veins than blood."</strong>
    </em>
  </p>
</blockquote><br><em>Thief</em> continues Caleb and Olivia's story, chronicling Caleb's unrelenting fight for Olivia. But this time Caleb speaks. He fights LIKE A BOSS and fights dirty. In fact, his methods reminded me of how dirty Olivia was in <em>The Opportunist</em> when she tried to win Caleb back. I thought this was interesting and showed just how similar these two actually are. Neither of them are perfect - not even our Caleb. The stunt Caleb pulled at dinner toward the beginning of the book had my jaw dropping on the floor in absolute shock. But that the same time, I was fist pumping him and cheering him on.<br><br>Underneath all their ugly lies is this beautiful burning love and intense connection - a connection that neither of them have had with anyone else, including their spouses. You could feel the electricity and the sparks between Olivia and Caleb. They didn't even need to be talking to each other. Their silence was enough to ignite the page and make it come alive. I loved every minute of it.<br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <em>
      <strong>“When I’m with you, every emotion I can possibly feel comes spilling out. I drown in them. I want to run to you, and I want to run away.” </strong>
    </em>
  </p>
</blockquote><br>Despite all their jackedupness, I loved seeing them together. I loved all their "isms". I loved that they used the code word "Peter Pan" when one of them wanted to know what the other was thinking. I loved that they held onto their penny after all these years. Olivia uses to word "hook me" Caleb when she wanted one of his special hugs. I loved that llamas reminded Caleb of Olivia from when they first met under a tree. Most of all I loved how deeply Caleb GOT Olivia and Olivia GOT Caleb. After the truth came out and the lies were erased, they were finally bared to each other.<br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <strong>
      <em>“I'll do whatever I have to do to protect you. I'll lie, cheat, and steal to make you okay. I'll share your suffering, and I'll carry you when you're weighed down. I'll never leave you, not even when you ask me to. Do you believe me?” </em>
    </strong>
  </p>
</blockquote><br>In true Tarryn Fisher fashion, Thief is not all sugary syrupy sweetness. There are no hearts, rainbows or unicorns. This was real life. Real life is messy. Love is messy. I appreciate how relatable this story was. <strong>Thief is an ode to first love, broken hearts and the hope for second chances.</strong><br><br>_________________________<br><br><strong>Find more of my reviews and other bookish things here:</strong><br><br><strong>✥ My blog <a href="http://readingbookslikeaboss.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">R</a><a href="http://readingbookslikeaboss.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">eading Books Like a Boss</a></strong><br><strong> ✥ Like on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/ReadingBooksLikeABoss" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a></strong><br><strong> ✥ Follow on <a href="http://twitter.com/ireadlikeaboss" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a></strong><br>_______________________________<br>Caleb's POV. "Thief" OMG!!!!!!! Do you know what this means? Do you? Do you? I don't either, but I'm all fired up!!! WAHOOOOOOOO!!!!!!<br><br>I'd really, really like to know when we can expect this masterpiece!! Until then, read the teasers below!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/622061.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/342679.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>04/01/2013</b><br>Teaser: The Penny<br>The door was slightly ajar when I arrived. I was about to knock when it swung open and a man came out carrying a garbage bag. I stepped back too startled to speak. My thoughts spun in a hundred directions. He wasn’t her type. I was going to kill him. Why was he taking out her trash? Did he sleep here often? I waited for him to look up, thinking every man deserved a chance to explain himself before he got the shit beat out of him. <br>He was mildly startled to see me standing in front of him. He looked past me to see if I was with someone else, and then said. <br>“Help you?”<br>He hadn’t pulled the door to Olivia’s apartment closed, and I could see inside. <br>Empty. <br>I felt the air leave my lungs. I closed my eyes tilting my head back. No, no, no. <br>I walked away, my hands in my hair and circled back to where maintenance was looking at me curiously. My instant jealousy had caused me to miss the uniform and name badge. Why had I left her? Why hadn’t I just stayed? I knew she did this. She ran when she was afraid. I thought—<br>What had I thought? That I could keep her because we’d made love? That her demons wouldn’t find her in the orange grove where I’d sold my soul to be with her? <br>I eyed the badge clipped to the front of his shirt. <br>“Miguel.” My voice sounded raw even to my ears. Miguel raised his eyebrows as he watched me struggle with a sentence. “When did she—? How long—?”<br>“This one’s been open for twenty four hours,” he said, referring to the apartment behind him. “We have a waiting list. Have to make it ready for next tenants.”<br>Twenty four hours? Where had she gone? Had she left right away? Had something scared her away? <br>I ran a hand through my hair. I’d left her just two days ago to go settle my affairs. I’d danced with her in the parking lot before I’d left. She’d tried to tell me the truth, but I’d stopped her. When she found out about the amnesia, she’d think of every possible reason to run from me. I’d planned on locking her in the apartment; making love to her again and convincing her that we could make it work. But, first I’d had loose ends to tie up. <br>I’d left Olivia and gone straight to Leah’s townhouse. When she opened the door I could tell she’d been crying. It took me thirty minutes to break her heart. It hurt me to do it. She had done nothing to deserve what I was doing to her. I told her I’d met someone. She didn’t ask who, though I suspected she knew since she’d followed me to Olivia’s apartment a few weeks earlier. Before I left, I kissed her forehead. I didn’t tell her about the amnesia. I didn’t want to hurt her any more than I already had. <br>I went to my condo next. As I stood under the shower I thought of our week together. I thought of the orange grove; of the way she tasted, the way her skin felt like cold satin beneath my fingers. When my mind went to that first moment of being inside her; of the way her eyes had widened and her lips had parted, I had to blast myself with cold water. <br>She’d given me everything—everything she’d held back before. She was different. She was also the same; stubborn, defiant...full of lies. <br>I’d tried to break her before. Now, I just wanted her as she was. I wanted every, last beautiful flaw. I wanted the witty one liner’s, and the coldness that only I knew how to warm. I wanted the fight and the friction and the make- up sex. I wanted her to wake up in my bed every morning. I wanted her shitty cooking and her beautiful, complex mind. <br>I’d gone back on everything I believed, to be with her. I threw truth out the window. I was so afraid she’d forget about me, I’d lied to sneak back into her life. Now, I had inordinate amounts of explaining to do. <br>I looked at Miguel. He suddenly seemed like my last remaining tie to her. <br>“Did she leave anything?—a note….anything?”<br>Miguel rubbed the back of his neck. “No, man.”<br>“Did she say where she was going?”<br>He sucked his teeth. “I’m just maintenance. They don’t exactly give me a forwarding address.” He looked around to make sure we were alone. “But, if she did leave something it would be in this black garbage bag, which I’m going to set right here while I do a run through of the apartment.”<br>He dropped the bag on the floor, and gave me a look before stepping back into the apartment and closing the door behind him. <br>I picked it up, weighed it in my hand. It was light. Had she left me something, telling me where she’d gone? Had Jim come back and scared her off? Had he told her? I knelt down and turned the bag over, dumping its contents on the concrete. I was sweating and my hands were damp as I sifted through the trash. Ripped up papers, broken glass, crushed flower petals….what was I looking for? A letter? Olivia would never write me a letter. It wasn’t her style. This was her style; leaving me without notice…throwing me in the fire to burn. I tossed the bag. Half of my heart was breaking, the other half was hell fucking angry. As the bag fluttered to the ground, I heard the slight tinkering of something hitting the floor. My eyes scanned the concrete, desperate for anything that would lead me to her. <br>I found it lying between my feet.<br> A penny. <br>Had she left it for me, or had she just left it? I picked it up, held it between my fingers. The once shiny surface had the slightly green tinge of aging copper. This was her goodbye? I felt anger and more than anger, I felt confusion. What had I done? The orange grove, the kiss in the parking lot before I’d left. I’d felt so sure of what I felt for her…what she felt for me. There was no way Olivia would have given herself to me if she wasn’t sure of us. Then why? <br>WHY?<br> I walked to the edge of the parking lot and lifted my fist, the penny pressing against my palm. Toss it. I told myself. My muscles tensed to throw it. <br>I couldn’t do it. My hand dropped to my side. I put the penny in my pocket and drove home. <br><br><br><b>02/22/2013<br><br><a href="http://www.maryse.net/news/tarryn-fishers-thief-teaser-caleb.html" rel="nofollow noopener">**THIEF TEASER HERE!!!!!**</a><br><br></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9446222985230244151" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer498732876" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11459512147009884774"><b>******* 6 EPIC STARS********</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“How many times can a heart be broken before it is beyond mend?".</i>
</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786130._SX540_.jpg' width='350' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786131.jpg' width='400' height='100' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><b>
  <i>“The day I met her under a tree, it was as if I breathed a spore of her into my lungs. We kept coming back to each other. The distance between our bodies grew wider over the years as we tried to live separately but the spore took root and grew.... Olivia is something that grows inside of me".~ Caleb Drake</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i> "Broken people give broken love. . . . And we are all a little broken. . . . .".<br/><br/><br/><i><b>This bo</b></i></i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText11459512147009884774" style="display:none"><b>******* 6 EPIC STARS********</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“How many times can a heart be broken before it is beyond mend?".</i>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786130._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786131.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><b>
  <i>“The day I met her under a tree, it was as if I breathed a spore of her into my lungs. We kept coming back to each other. The distance between our bodies grew wider over the years as we tried to live separately but the spore took root and grew.... Olivia is something that grows inside of me".~ Caleb Drake</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i> "Broken people give broken love. . . . And we are all a little broken. . . . .".<br><br><br><i><b>This book....</b></i></i>
</b> *shakes head* <i>this book</i> is the perfect verse over tight beat.<br><br><b>Tarryn Fisher's</b> writing is so raw, rare, elegant and rhythmical -it penetrates through to your skin, runs through your veins and pierces your heart. It flows so naturally and it’s so addictive that it will leave you desperately hungry for more. You will find yourself rereading each sentence over and over and over again. I feared blinking incase I'd missing something. I was fighting to absorb it all in, in hope of storing those words for keepsake in my memory bank. I had to restrain myself from highlighting the entire book and quoting it in my status updates. <i>(I think I did right?)</i> Every sentence is more powerful than the next.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786132.png" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Fix You" By Cold Play </i>
</b>was playing on repeat on my IPod while reading - no song could have portayed this series better. <i>Tarryn Fisher</i> play list for the series included a lot of Cold Play and "Fix You" was also mentioned. The lyrics are so breathtaking and I have included them throughout my review!<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=pY9b6jgbNyc">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=pY9b6j...</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786133.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is about the obsessive kind of love that can destroy you and everything around it. You know it's bad for you but there's not a damn thing you can do to make go away and what's worse is that you don't ever want it to go away- <i>ever!</i> Their lack of communication, courage and misunderstandings not only destroyed them but anyone else that came into contact with them emotionally. There was <b>always</b> something stopping them from being together whether it was timing, lies, pride, or misunderstandings. It was heartbreaking to witness them make the same mistakes over and over and over again. It's a vicious cycle that had me begging <b> *begging* </b> for it to end to the point where it became unbearable and I was certain I couldn't possibly handle anymore pain.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786134.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <br><i>
  <b>“She will be your destruction. She's not healthy”. - Luca <br><br>"Then let her destroy me". ~ Caleb Kaspen </b>
</i> <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786135.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br><br><b>
  <u>Olivia Kaspen</u>
</b> <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786136.jpg" width="350" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Caleb Drake</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786137._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>“She has the kind of love that can stain your soul, make you beg not to have one, just to escape the spell she’s put you under. I’ve tried to break myself of her over and over, but it’s pointless. I’ve got more of her in my veins than blood”. ~ Caleb Drake </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786138.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Tarryn fisher</i> has a distinct way of cracking your chest open, baring your soul, ripping your heart out, stomping on it and in that single second before you feel like you’re about to take your last breath she shoves it back in your chest. You survive, but your heart will never be the same again. She is an extraordinarily gifted author, who not only thinks outside the box but also challenges the reader to do the same. The originality and uniqueness of her work will leave you speechless and awe struck. The effort that she has put into her work is evident through the flawless details and the well thought out puzzles. To me, this book is like a riddle that required solving- you actually need to exercise your brain to try solving the answers. It's an exhausting yet liberating experience and I have truly enjoyed every second of it. I will remember this book forever!<br><br><br><br>This story slowly skinned the barriers around my heart until it was left bare, vulnerable and bleeding- it was brutal! I'm an emotional person but I don't cry often. I take pain until it leaves me feeling choked up. <i>This book broke me</i>- it was a first for me. I’m not talking about shedding a tear or a two either; I’m talking about ugly splotchy sobbing like baby while your chest heaves crying - <b>not-a-pretty-sight!</b> It wasn’t one specific scene that caused this, it was the intensity of it all and the slow build up of the suffering they endured which left me feeling hopeless, raw and led me to the point of breaking down. <i>
  <b>(Are you sure you don’t have some strands of dirty red in your hair Tarryn???)</b>
</i> *wink*<br><br><i>
  <b>A single sob escapes her lips "You got married ....and had a baby...." Her tears are flowing freely, mingling with her mascara and tracking black across her cheeks."You were supposed to marry me. That was supposed to be my baby”. Her tiny frame racks with sobs.~ Olivia Kaspen</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404021ra/786139.gif" width="350" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The first book in the series <i>The Opportunist</i> was the puzzle- it was the foundation of the series. All the answers are there but they are blind to the naked eye. If you look at it from the surface you would blame Caleb, but if you really take a moment to dig deeper and allow your mind to think outside of the box you would discover there's so much more that meets the eye. You will come up with so many theories, excuses and 'what ifs' that you will start to feel like you're going insane. The foundation in <i>The Opportunist </i>had so many cracks in it, that there was no way to restore it, it was at the point of no return. All you could do was make an attempt at putting the pieces to together, make assumptions and hope that one day it can bare the weight of something more.<br><br>To some extent, <i>Dirty Red </i>filled in those cracks, it was essential to the story as it explains how those cracks surfaced in the first place. It was written in Leah's POV <b>- although personally, I preferred to call her Gingerpubs-skank-bitch-she-devil!!!</b><br><br>In <i>Thief</i>, although the foundation has been mildly restored, it is not perfect and the building on that foundation is a slow long painful process resulting in a not so perfect result. This book was perfection- <b>period!</b> I felt like Inspector Gadget when I was reading it. I found myself constantly lingering on a page and rereading each sentence. I was dissecting each word, sentence, expression, breaking it down into tiny little pieces and then going back to beginning to see if that theory fits. In the end, the picture to that puzzle was heartbreakly beautiful. <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786140.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br> <br>The story alternates between past and present filling in the gaps to unanswered questions in <i>The Opportunist</i>. It will shock you, make you scream, cry and make you feel like someone has punched you in the gut and knocked the air out of you. <b>Angst</b> is not the word to describe this book.. It's <i>torture</i>, pure slow torture and I <i>felt</i> every little inch of it. The detail that was used blew my mind. Tarryn grabs you by your both arms and yanks you into this story. I <i>felt, breathed</i> and <i>lived</i> these characters for a short period but their journey will stay will me forever. Her detailed description of emotions, mannerisms, facial expressions, reactions, what the characters wore <i>(I wonder if that emerald green dress comes in my size?)</i> the love scenes that were one of the most tasteful sexy scenes I've ever read.. all of it! There's simply too many moments to list - If I did, I'd end up writing my own book on what I loved about this book! <br><br>I *loved* all the endearing references that were made like Peter Pan, The Orange Grove, Jaxsons, the Ilama, upper cut me, the Penny, Duchess, the Deflated Basket Ball, it all gave it that extra special something – <i>it was the cherry on top of the Cherry Garcia!</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786141.jpg" width="300" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>Now for the end-</i> As I've mentioned (many many times) there was a point in the book the pain was so unbearable I remember messaging my poor book buddy Nikki (while she was on vacation mind you) and telling her that it was <i>"Hopeless, there would be no f*cking light and it was unfixable".</i> I love a fairy tale story, who doesn't right? However, their story was anything but perfect. Their story was flawed, it had sharp thorns that cut deep and left a stain and therefore their ending was so fitting. There were so many mistakes made, so much pain and hurt caused. <i>As Cammie said,</i> <b>
  <i>"There wasn't just water under their bridge. there was maggots, shit and dead bodies".</i>
</b>A fairy tale ending would have seemed so ridiculous at that point and I just don't think that's Tarryn’s style. Without trying to ruin the story, I will say this- the ending was a <i>flawed HEA</i>. I believed it was perfect for them and I was content with it. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I think that Olivia miscarrying and not being able to have children is almost like Karma for how all this started. The very first lie of when she took Jessica to her the abortion. It was almost like her penance for it.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>Despite all the pain Tarryn put me through, I don't regret a <b>single second</b> of it. I feel honored to have had the opportunity to read such a brilliant life altering story. This is a <b>MUST</b> read <b>NOW</b> story! Books like this one <i>right here</i>, are what stem my absolute love for reading.<br><br>This is by far the <b>best book </b> I have read this year and I will be re reading it . . . <i>
  <b>"Again and again and again and again".</b>
</i> <br><br><i>Bravo Tarryn Fisher!</i><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786142.jpg" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786143._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br><i>
  <b>"She is the only woman I see..." ~ Thief~ Caleb Drake</b>
</i> <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404021i/786144.png" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br><br><i>* Buddy Read with Nikki <i></i>- Kenikki, Thanks for putting up with my midnight heart stopping rantings while you were trying to relax on vacation!!! At least it was a vacation you will never forget, right? *wink*</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha">SueBee★bring me an alpha!★</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer489144658" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8995406717064685949"><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/FisherThief3TitlebySueBee_zpse9695e9e.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402576i/782570.jpg' alt=' photo FisherThief3TitlebySueBee_zpse9695e9e.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★★! Love Me With Lies, book 3 of 3! The conclusion of Caleb’s & Olivia’s epic & very dysfunctional love!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“She has the kind of love that can stain your soul, make you beg not to have one, just to escape the spell she’s put you under. I’ve tried to break myself of her over and over, but it’s pointless. I’ve got more of her in my veins than blood.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><b>The Love Me With Lies series is Caleb Drake’s and Olivia Kaspen’s whirlwind saga spanning over a decade</b> filled with love, j</span>
  <span id="freeText8995406717064685949" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/FisherThief3TitlebySueBee_zpse9695e9e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402576i/782570.jpg" alt=" photo FisherThief3TitlebySueBee_zpse9695e9e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★★! Love Me With Lies, book 3 of 3! The conclusion of Caleb’s &amp; Olivia’s epic &amp; very dysfunctional love!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“She has the kind of love that can stain your soul, make you beg not to have one, just to escape the spell she’s put you under. I’ve tried to break myself of her over and over, but it’s pointless. I’ve got more of her in my veins than blood.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>The Love Me With Lies series is Caleb Drake’s and Olivia Kaspen’s whirlwind saga spanning over a decade</b> filled with love, joy, angst, anger, frustration, but mostly a <b>profound sadness for all the could-have-beens</b>. Their love, in all its dysfunction and deception, is so great it blurs the line between right and wrong, overcomes trial and tribulation with hopes of transcending time!<br><br><u>Books in Love Me With Lies series should be read in order and together:</u><br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484477044" rel="nofollow noopener">The Opportunist</a> (book 1)<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489144410" rel="nofollow noopener">Dirty Red</a> (book 2)<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489144658" rel="nofollow noopener">Thief</a> (book 3)</b><br><br><b>Thief (book 3) is the final installment in the Love Me With Lies trilogy</b>. In the previous two books we got to know Olivia and the Leah, the villain. <b>This is Caleb’s story</b>. It covers the events from <b>his POV from the beginning to the end, spanning some fifteen years</b>. We finally get clarification as the final pieces in the puzzle that has been Caleb’s and Olivia’s whirlwind romance are put in place. Be prepared for yet another <b>roller-coaster of lies, deceit, misunderstandings, set-back and above all self-sabotage….</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/FisherLovemewithlies1-3HeroinebySueBee_zps51a1c7ec.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401890i/780603.jpg" alt=" photo FisherLovemewithlies1-3HeroinebySueBee_zps51a1c7ec.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Olivia has matured over the years. Five words to describe <b>Olivia: Resilient, broken, insightful, endearing and focused</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“When I’m with you, every emotion I can possibly feel comes spilling out. I drown in them. I want to run to you, and I want to run away.” ~ Olivia</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/FisherLovemewithlies1-3HerobySueBee_zpsfb630566.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401890i/780604.jpg" alt=" photo FisherLovemewithlies1-3HerobySueBee_zpsfb630566.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Finally we get to know the enigma that has been Caleb. As it turns out it didn’t find him very deceptive and I just love him more for it. Five words to describe <b>Caleb: Captivating, enigmatic, unforgettable, determined and enduring</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I knew I was lying to myself by thinking I could fix her. But, it was too late. I didn’t know how to let go.” ~ Caleb</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>I can’t recall when last I felt such an urge to see a hero/heroine together!</b> It’s a bittersweet HEA for me. My heart has been broken so many times over it's splintered. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Mostly for two reasons; one for all the years wasted and two because when they finally found their way back to each they one thing they really wanted they could never have… <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <b>Ms. Fisher’s writing is exquisite and the series plot has been most unusual, fresh and superbly executed. Spellbinding! Unforgettable! Unique! Epic!</b> Thanks Ms. Fisher! <br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Life does not accommodate you, it shatters you. Love is mean, but it’s good. It keeps us alive. If you need her, then wait. But, right now she’s getting married. It’s her day and you can’t ruin it.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5 stars <br>Heroine rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 4 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 3.5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 5 stars<br>Storyline execution rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: 3.5<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 5 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Yes.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Problems/tumblr_mobvx7vqsM1s087b2o1_500_zpse85f9b77.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402576ra/782571.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mobvx7vqsM1s087b2o1_500_zpse85f9b77.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer541998881" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer18305172073226759056">“She will be your destruction. She's not healthy."<br/>I gently removed her hand from my arm. "Then let her destroy me.” <br/><br/>5 STARS *****<br/><br/>CALEB DRAKE. There is a reason he sits in my top five favorite book boyfriends of all time, and this book was the perfect example why. Prepare to swoon ladies! Prepare to swoon!<br/><br/>CALEB<br/><a href='http://imgur.com/v4Iicbl' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410553i/805171.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Now, I love imperfect characters and imperfect stories. Books that surprise, feel unexpected and original - and Tarryn Fisher has delivered exactly that with the LOVE ME WITH LIES SERIE</span>
  <span id="freeText18305172073226759056" style="display:none">“She will be your destruction. She's not healthy."<br>I gently removed her hand from my arm. "Then let her destroy me.” <br><br>5 STARS *****<br><br>CALEB DRAKE. There is a reason he sits in my top five favorite book boyfriends of all time, and this book was the perfect example why. Prepare to swoon ladies! Prepare to swoon!<br><br>CALEB<br><a href="http://imgur.com/v4Iicbl" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410553i/805171.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Now, I love imperfect characters and imperfect stories. Books that surprise, feel unexpected and original - and Tarryn Fisher has delivered exactly that with the LOVE ME WITH LIES SERIES! It's something that is a little different from the norm. Flawed characters that are completely relatable in their own way. I adore every one of them, including the villain, Leah. <br>Her stories aren't sugary sweet, and not wrapped up in a fairytale bow - and that is what I truly love. I need it - I crave it! It's what makes her one of my favorite authors of all time.<br><br>OLIVIA (as per Tarryn Fisher's PINTEREST page - she loves Natalie Dormer as Olivia)<br><a href="http://imgur.com/aCZm7wN" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410553ra/805172.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Now telling you about THIEF would really spoil the rollercoaster and experience for you... its better to talk a big gulp of air and jump into the pure hotness that is Caleb Drake and get completely wrapped up in his present and his past as the story unfolds and reconnects with THE OPPORTUNIST and DIRTY RED. <br><br>But know this...<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/HDWja5O" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410553i/805173.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>ITS ALL JUST - <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/wCiSj4e" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410553ra/805174.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>5 CALEB DRAKE LOVING STARS!! *****<br><br>and PS... <br>* Tarryn Fisher * I can't wait to see what you write next!!!! <br>Love your work!!!<br><br></span>

<div id="review_467001640" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/467001640" />
    <a title="~IreneOust~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13784133-ireneoust"><img alt="~IreneOust~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1350753189p2/13784133.jpg" /></a>

<span id="freeTextContainer8086530480510855194"><br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=2vskq5g' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399288i/772503.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>To give this book a 5* rating was one of the easiest decidions I ever made!<br/><br/>This trilogy was one of several <i>firsts</i> for me ...<br/><br/><b>Opportunist</b> made me pull my first all-nighter and made me cry over a book [as an audlt] for the first time.<br/><br/><b>Dirty Red</b> was the first book I loved where I loathed the main character.<br/><br/><b>Thief</b> was the first book that made me realize that doing the right thing isn't always the best thing and being a little selfish isn't always such a bad thing.<br/><br/>This was such an emotional journey </span>
  <span id="freeText8086530480510855194" style="display:none"><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2vskq5g" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>To give this book a 5* rating was one of the easiest decidions I ever made!<br><br>This trilogy was one of several <i>firsts</i> for me ...<br><br><b>Opportunist</b> made me pull my first all-nighter and made me cry over a book [as an audlt] for the first time.<br><br><b>Dirty Red</b> was the first book I loved where I loathed the main character.<br><br><b>Thief</b> was the first book that made me realize that doing the right thing isn't always the best thing and being a little selfish isn't always such a bad thing.<br><br>This was such an emotional journey [for me] and the fact that it's over makes me really sad. I've grown to know and love these characters &amp; all of their flaws. <br><br>In true Tarryn's fashion, the ending was <i>almost</i> perfect and I wouldn't have it any other way.<br><br><br><br><i>Where there is desire<br>There is gonna be a flame<br>Where there is a flame<br>Someone's bound to get burned<br>But just because it burns<br>Doesn't mean you're gonna die<br>You've gotta get up and try, and try, and try ... </i><br><br>Pink<br>from <i>Try</i><br><br><br><br>*** Finally a book from Caleb's POV I actually enjoyed ;)<br> </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8535176980612284679">4.5 STARS!<br/><a href='https://ibb.co/x3fzMXc' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1578390030ra/28729158.gif' alt='Thief' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>📚 “𝑩𝒓𝒐𝒌𝒆𝒏 𝒑𝒆𝒐𝒑𝒍𝒆 𝒈𝒊𝒗𝒆 𝒃𝒓𝒐𝒌𝒆𝒏 𝒍𝒐𝒗𝒆. 𝑨𝒏𝒅 𝒘𝒆 𝒂𝒓𝒆 𝒂𝒍𝒍 𝒂 𝒍𝒊𝒕𝒕𝒍𝒆 𝒃𝒓𝒐𝒌𝒆𝒏.” 📚<br/><br/>This book scared me to death... I mean, come on, Tarryn Fisher is known as crazy and unpredictable, so I was VERY worried for the fate of her characters and I had no idea how the book would end. 😱😂<br/>'Thief' is written from Caleb's point of view. The plot continues the second book, which ends with Leah's crazy discovery. 💥<br/><br/>Caleb is determined to win the girl who broke his heart - and he doesn't care about the conseque</span>
  <span id="freeText8535176980612284679" style="display:none">4.5 STARS!<br><a href="https://ibb.co/x3fzMXc" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1578390030ra/28729158.gif" alt="Thief" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>📚 “𝑩𝒓𝒐𝒌𝒆𝒏 𝒑𝒆𝒐𝒑𝒍𝒆 𝒈𝒊𝒗𝒆 𝒃𝒓𝒐𝒌𝒆𝒏 𝒍𝒐𝒗𝒆. 𝑨𝒏𝒅 𝒘𝒆 𝒂𝒓𝒆 𝒂𝒍𝒍 𝒂 𝒍𝒊𝒕𝒕𝒍𝒆 𝒃𝒓𝒐𝒌𝒆𝒏.” 📚<br><br>This book scared me to death... I mean, come on, Tarryn Fisher is known as crazy and unpredictable, so I was VERY worried for the fate of her characters and I had no idea how the book would end. 😱😂<br>'Thief' is written from Caleb's point of view. The plot continues the second book, which ends with Leah's crazy discovery. 💥<br><br>Caleb is determined to win the girl who broke his heart - and he doesn't care about the consequences ... 😱<br>They haven't met in months, but like in the previous books - they always find their way to each other and always leave a trail of destruction and heartbreak behind them.<br>If you ask me? It's not a novel... it's a TRAGEDY!!! 💔💔💔<br><br>📚 “𝑰 𝒅𝒐𝒏’𝒕 𝒈𝒆𝒕 𝒕𝒐 𝒃𝒆 𝒘𝒊𝒕𝒉 𝒉𝒆𝒓. 𝑰 𝒋𝒖𝒔𝒕 𝒅𝒐𝒏’𝒕 𝒘𝒂𝒏𝒕 𝒕𝒐 𝒃𝒆 𝒘𝒊𝒕𝒉 𝒂𝒏𝒚𝒐𝒏𝒆 𝒆𝒍𝒔𝒆.” 📚<br><br>Tarryn has done an amazing job of explaining Caleb's actions in the past. In my opinion, the choice to end the series from Caleb's point of view was ingenious, because I definitely wanted to know what drew him to Olivia or Leah in the first place ... ❤<br><br>Caleb's perspective also changed everything I thought I knew about the plot and everything I read in the previous two books! <br>If I liked Caleb, after this book, I absolutely LOVE HIM !!! 😍❤<br>His feelings are so strong and powerful. He knows exactly what he wants and he doesn't give up - so how can you not fall in love with him ??? 💋<br><br>📚 ”𝑰’𝒗𝒆 𝒏𝒆𝒗𝒆𝒓 𝒍𝒐𝒗𝒆𝒅 𝒂𝒏𝒚𝒐𝒏𝒆 𝒂𝒇𝒕𝒆𝒓 𝒚𝒐𝒖. 𝑰 𝒏𝒆𝒗𝒆𝒓 𝒘𝒊𝒍𝒍.” 📚<br><br>However, in my opinion the first book was most surprising, but this book was definitely over too quickly for my liking ... 😬<br>So if you love original and unexpected love stories, you have to read this series!!! 👑😱<br><br>▪️▫️▪️▫️▪️▫️▪️▫️▪️▫️▪️▫️▪️▫️▪️▫️<br><br>📖 ᖴOᒪᒪOᗯ ᗰE Oᑎ IᑎᔕTᗩGᖇᗩᗰ: 🎉 <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.instagram.com/the_romantic_blogger/">https://www.instagram.com/the_romanti...</a><br><br>📖 ᐯIᔕIT ᗰY ᗷᒪOG ᖴOᖇ ᗰOᖇE ᖇEᐯIEᗯᔕ: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://books-romance.com/">https://books-romance.com/</a></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/448218433" />
    <a title="Claire Contreras" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10054133-claire-contreras"><img alt="Claire Contreras" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544066540p2/10054133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/448218433?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Claire Contreras" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Claire Contreras" href="/user/show/10054133-claire-contreras">Claire Contreras</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10054133-claire-contreras?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer448218433" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9494391933800295252">I highlighted SO much of this book, but I don't want to post my favorite quotes on here :(. I want to wrap them up and keep them to myself so that I can open them on a dark gloomy day and read them over and cry. <br/><br/>I do this thing when I read, and I wish I wouldn't, but I do, where I analyze the crap out of sentences, words, phrases and the way they're used. It's a strange little habit I've developed over the years. Sometimes when I read, I find myself doing that more than enjoying the actual story</span>
  <span id="freeText9494391933800295252" style="display:none">I highlighted SO much of this book, but I don't want to post my favorite quotes on here :(. I want to wrap them up and keep them to myself so that I can open them on a dark gloomy day and read them over and cry. <br /><br />I do this thing when I read, and I wish I wouldn't, but I do, where I analyze the crap out of sentences, words, phrases and the way they're used. It's a strange little habit I've developed over the years. Sometimes when I read, I find myself doing that more than enjoying the actual story, and that pisses me off. I do that with Tarryn's books too, but she does this thing with her words and she makes me get lost in them. I drown in them and I feel the need to stay submerged and let them consume every part of me forever. <br /><br />THAT.<br /><br />Is talent.<br /><br />THAT.<br /><br />Is a <i> real </i> writer. <br /><br />THAT.<br /><br />Is a gift.<br /><br />I loved this book. I loved it more so than The Opportunist. Not only because my heart hurt as much as it did when I read TO, but because Tarryn's writing grew. It did. I promise. As difficult as it is to wrap your mind around the fact that brilliant writing could grow MORE, it did. <br /><br />I loved every. single. heart breaking part about this story. I loved every. single. beautiful part about this book. Every. single. soul staining part of it. <br /><br />All the Peter Pans, all the Duchesses and Cherry Garcias and even the Dirty Reds, will stay with me forever. <br /><br />Thank you, Fisher. You did good. You did good :). <br /><br /><b> I've grown attached to my broken heart. I think I'll keep it. </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9494391933800295252" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1509664795" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1509664795" />
    <a title="Beth Hudspeth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18107143-beth-hudspeth"><img alt="Beth Hudspeth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1495723320p2/18107143.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1509664795?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth Hudspeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth Hudspeth" href="/user/show/18107143-beth-hudspeth">Beth Hudspeth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18107143-beth-hudspeth?shelf=book-reviews">book-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18107143-beth-hudspeth?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1509664795" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15817902828894724191">Okay, maybe I am a nutcase along with Olivia, Leah and Caleb because I am so addicted...<br/><br/>Finally we get into Caleb's head and after Leah's book I welcomed that with open arms.<br/><br/><b>“How many times can a heart be broken before it is beyond mend?”</b> I DON'T KNOW TARRYN FISHER HOW MANY TIMES ARE YOU WILLING TO BREAK IT?! My heart felt broken in a few different ways, but by the ending it felt like it started to mend.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453084405ra/17779234.gif' alt=' photo never let me go_zps2rsswgwr.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Caleb is fighting to win Olivia back. Thief takes us back through the journey of their story </span>
  <span id="freeText15817902828894724191" style="display:none">Okay, maybe I am a nutcase along with Olivia, Leah and Caleb because I am so addicted...<br><br>Finally we get into Caleb's head and after Leah's book I welcomed that with open arms.<br><br><b>“How many times can a heart be broken before it is beyond mend?”</b> I DON'T KNOW TARRYN FISHER HOW MANY TIMES ARE YOU WILLING TO BREAK IT?! My heart felt broken in a few different ways, but by the ending it felt like it started to mend.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453084405ra/17779234.gif" alt=" photo never let me go_zps2rsswgwr.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Caleb is fighting to win Olivia back. Thief takes us back through the journey of their story of lies, jealousy and love through Caleb's eyes and it was so nice to see just how much he loves Olivia. There were times when I didn't really trust his feelings for her or his sincerity, but after reading this those feelings have been put to rest. There has been no one else that has been able to take his mind off of her for 10 years. This was a tug of war with my emotions, I wanted them to do the right thing for each other.<br><br>Thief felt like it didn't belong with the other two, same characters but I didn't really hate them AS much, except for Leah "Dirty Red".. she is awful and can rot in hell. We didn't really get a lot of her which was fine with me. Even without her presence as known she still managed to make me hate her even more! She is a vile human. Olivia seems to have matured a little bit and has gotten over some issues in her life. She was much more likable to me in Thief. I LOVED Caleb in this. He had his sights set and wasn't giving up.<br><br><b>“She will be your destruction. She's not healthy."<br>"Then let her destroy me.”</b><br><br><b>“Lies, it sounds demented to want a woman’s lies. But, Olivia loves you with her lies. She lies about how she’s feeling, how she’s hurting, how she wants you when she tells you she doesn’t. She lies to protect you and herself.”</b> This sort of helped me understand why Caleb loves Olivia so much. It helped me understand why she is so standoffish and why she does what she does. This is really one dysfunctional relationship, but I love them!<br><br>My favorite part of the whole book...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453084405ra/17779235.gif" alt=" photo hannaslapsjenna_zps4iqq7iet.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>YES OLIVIA, YES GIRL!</i><br><br>This series is one I will be thinking about for a while. It will be hard to get the characters our of my head. Every time I see Cherry Garcia ice cream, a souvenir penny machine, Peter Pan, Airport Blue or a really pretty tree I will be thinking about Olivia and Caleb. <br><br><b>I fell in love under a tree.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15817902828894724191" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

And in a certain way it was: a completely awesome and f***ed up journey. <br>And I loved every single second of it. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403395ra/784775.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Life isn’t always pretty.
